<h2 id="learnhub-e-learning-website---complete-technical-documentation"><strong>LEARNHUB E-LEARNING WEBSITE - Complete Technical Documentation</strong></h2>
<p>Based on my comprehensive analysis of your GitHub repository, here's everything about your project:</p>
<hr>
<h2 id="-executive-summary"><strong>📋 Executive Summary</strong></h2>
<p><strong>LearnHub</strong> is a modern, professional e-learning platform built with <strong>React 19</strong>, featuring a responsive course marketplace with shopping cart functionality. The platform showcases advanced React patterns, state management using Context API, and a sophisticated UI with glassmorphism design.</p>
<p><strong>Repository:</strong> <a href="https://github.com/Rohith-180503/LEARNHUB-E-LEARNING-WEBSITE">https://github.com/Rohith-180503/LEARNHUB-E-LEARNING-WEBSITE</a><br>
<strong>Live Demo:</strong> <a href="https://rohith-180503.github.io/LEARNHUB-E-LEARNING-WEBSITE/">https://rohith-180503.github.io/LEARNHUB-E-LEARNING-WEBSITE/</a><br>
<strong>Language Composition:</strong> JavaScript (66%), CSS (33.6%), HTML (0.4%)</p>
<hr>
<h2 id="-project-overview"><strong>📊 PROJECT OVERVIEW</strong></h2>
<h3 id="core-features"><strong>Core Features</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li>✅ 44+ Courses across 8+ categories</li>
<li>✅ Dynamic Shopping Cart with persistent storage</li>
<li>✅ Responsive Design (Mobile, Tablet, Desktop)</li>
<li>✅ Dark Mode / Light Mode Toggle</li>
<li>✅ Advanced Navigation with Dropdowns</li>
<li>✅ Toast Notifications (React Toastify)</li>
<li>✅ Professional Styling with Glassmorphism</li>
<li>✅ Unit Testing (Vitest + React Testing Library)</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<h3 id="state-management"><strong>State Management</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>React Context API</strong> - Global Cart Management</li>
<li><strong>useContext Hook</strong> - Consume Context</li>
<li><strong>useMemo &amp; useCallback</strong> - Performance Optimization</li>
<li><strong>localStorage API</strong> - Cart Persistence</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="styling"><strong>Styling</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li>Pure CSS3 with Custom Properties (CSS Variables)</li>
<li>Flexbox &amp; CSS Grid</li>
<li>Media Queries for Responsive Design</li>
<li>Glassmorphism Design Pattern</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="-application-architecture"><strong>🎯 APPLICATION ARCHITECTURE</strong></h2>
<h3 id="layered-architecture-pattern"><strong>Layered Architecture Pattern</strong></h3>
<pre><code>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    UI/Presentation Layer            │
���    Pages (Home, Content Pages, Explore)             │
│                                                     │
│  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│  │        Components Layer                       │ │
│  │   ┌──────────┐  ┌───────────┐  ┌──────────┐ │ │
│  │   │ Navbar   │  │ Cart      │  │ Course   │ │ │
│  │   │Component │  │ Component │  │ Component│ │ │
│  │   └──────────┘  └───────────┘  └──────────┘ │ │
│  └───────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                     │
│  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│  │    State Management &amp; Logic Layer             │ │
│  │   ┌────────────────────────────────────────┐ │ │
│  │   │  CartContext.jsx (Context API)         │ │ │
│  │   │  - addToCart()                         │ │ │
│  │   │  - removeFromCart()                    │ │ │
│  │   │  - clearCart()                         │ │ │
│  │   └────────────────────────────────────────┘ │ │
│  └───────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                     │
│  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│  │    Data Layer                                │ │
│  │   ┌────────────────────────────────────────┐ │ │
│  │   │  fakeData.js (44 Mock Courses)         │ │ │
│  │   │  localStorage (Cart Persistence)       │ │ │
│  │   └────────────────────────────────────────┘ │ │
│  └───────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
│                                                     │
│  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
│  │    Styling Layer                             │ │
│  │   App.css, index.css, Component CSS files   │ │
│  └───────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

         ↓ React Router DOM ↓
         Client-Side Routing
</code></pre>
<h3 id="data-flow-diagram"><strong>Data Flow Diagram</strong></h3>
<pre><code>User Interaction
     ↓
Navbar / Course Component
     ↓
Event Handler (onClick)
     ↓
CartContext Methods
(addToCart, removeFromCart)
     ↓
State Update (setCart)
     ↓
useEffect triggers
     ↓
localStorage.setItem() → Persist Data
     ↓
Component Re-render
     ↓
UI Updated with new Cart
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2 id="-key-components"><strong>🔑 KEY COMPONENTS</strong></h2>
<h3 id="1-cartcontextjsx---state-management-brain"><strong>1. CartContext.jsx - State Management Brain</strong></h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-title class_">Purpose</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Global</span> cart state management using <span class="hljs-title class_">React</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Context</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">API</span>

<span class="hljs-title class_">Key</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Features</span>:
✓ <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span> integration <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> persistence
✓ useCallback <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> memoized functions
✓ useMemo <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> computed values
✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span> handling <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> storage quota

<span class="hljs-title class_">Exports</span>:
- <span class="hljs-title class_">CartProvider</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Wrapper</span> component
- <span class="hljs-attr">useCart</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Custom</span> hook <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> accessing cart

<span class="hljs-title class_">State</span>:
- <span class="hljs-attr">cart</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Array</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">of</span> course objects
- <span class="hljs-attr">cartCount</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Number</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">of</span> courses
- <span class="hljs-attr">cartTotal</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Sum</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">of</span> prices

<span class="hljs-title class_">Methods</span>:
- <span class="hljs-title function_">addToCart</span>(course): <span class="hljs-title class_">Add</span> course <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> not duplicate
- <span class="hljs-title function_">removeFromCart</span>(id): <span class="hljs-title class_">Remove</span> specific course
- <span class="hljs-title function_">clearCart</span>(): <span class="hljs-title class_">Empty</span> the cart
</code></pre>
<h3 id="2-navbarjsx---navigation-hub-186kb"><strong>2. Navbar.jsx - Navigation Hub (18.6KB)</strong></h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-title class_">Purpose</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Master</span> navigation <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> dropdowns, cart panel, theme toggle

<span class="hljs-title class_">Key</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Features</span>:

✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Dark</span> mode / <span class="hljs-title class_">Light</span> mode toggle
✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Cart</span> panel <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> pricing breakdown

- <span class="hljs-title class_">Logo</span> + <span class="hljs-title class_">Branding</span>
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Navigation</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Links</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> dropdowns
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Theme</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Toggle</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Button</span>

- <span class="hljs-title class_">Cart</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Slide</span>-out <span class="hljs-title class_">Panel</span>

<span class="hljs-title class_">State</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Management</span>:
- <span class="hljs-attr">mobileOpen</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Mobile</span> menu state
- <span class="hljs-attr">activeDropdown</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Which</span> dropdown is open

<h3 id="3-cartjsx---shopping-cart-display"><strong>3. Cart.jsx - Shopping Cart Display</strong></h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-title class_">Purpose</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Display</span> all enrolled courses <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> remove buttons

<span class="hljs-title class_">Features</span>:

✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Total</span> price calculation

✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Empty</span> state handling

<span class="hljs-title class_">Displays</span>:
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Cart</span> title <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> icon
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Course</span> count badge
- <span class="hljs-title class_">List</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">of</span> courses <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> instructor &amp; price
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Remove</span> buttons <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> each course
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Estimated</span> total <span class="hljs-keyword">with</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">fixed</span>(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>) precision
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Checkout</span> &amp; <span class="hljs-title class_">Clear</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Cart</span> buttons
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Back</span> to catalog link
</code></pre>

<h3 id="responsive-breakpoints"><strong>Responsive Breakpoints</strong></h3>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* Mobile First Approach */</span>
- Mobile: &lt; <span class="hljs-number">576px</span> (<span class="hljs-number">100%</span> width, single column)
- Tablet: <span class="hljs-number">576px</span> - <span class="hljs-number">992px</span> (<span class="hljs-number">2</span>-<span class="hljs-number">3</span> columns)
- Desktop: &gt; <span class="hljs-number">992px</span> (<span class="hljs-number">4</span>+ columns, full UI)
- Ultra-wide: &gt; <span class="hljs-number">1400px</span> (<span class="hljs-number">6</span>+ columns)
</code></pre>
<h3 id="design-patterns"><strong>Design Patterns</strong></h3>
<p><strong>1. Glassmorphism</strong> (Dropdown menus, Cart panel)</p>
<pre><code class="language-css">backdrop-<span class="hljs-attribute">filter</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">blur</span>(<span class="hljs-number">10px</span>);
<span class="hljs-attribute">background</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">rgba</span>(<span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.1</span>);
<span class="hljs-attribute">border</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1px</span> solid <span class="hljs-built_in">rgba</span>(<span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.2</span>);
</code></pre>
<p><strong>2. Flexbox Grid</strong> (Course cards, Navbar)</p>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-attribute">display</span>: flex;
<span class="hljs-attribute">flex-wrap</span>: wrap;
<span class="hljs-attribute">gap</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1rem</span>;
<span class="hljs-attribute">justify-content</span>: space-between;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>3. Dark Mode</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-selector-tag">body</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.dark-mode</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attr">--bg-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#1a202c</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attr">--text-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#f7fafc</span>;
}
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2 id="-data-flow--state-management"><strong>🔄 DATA FLOW &amp; STATE MANAGEMENT</strong></h2>
<h3 id="complete-user-journey"><strong>Complete User Journey</strong></h3>
<pre><code>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ User visits /                               │
│ App.jsx renders                             │
│ CartProvider wraps everything               │
│ Navbar + Home page loaded                   │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘
               ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ Loads fakeData (44 courses)                 │
│ Maps courses to Course components           │
│ Each course card has &quot;Add to cart&quot; button    │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘
               ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ User clicks &quot;Add to cart&quot;                   │
│ Course.jsx → handleEnroll()                 │
│ Calls useCart().addToCart(course)           │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘
               ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ CartContext.addToCart()                     │
│ Validates: not duplicate?                   │
│ Updates state: setCart([...prev, course])   │
│ Toast notification: &quot;Added to cart&quot;         │
└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────┘
               ↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ useEffect triggers                          │
│ localStorage.setItem('learnhub-cart', ...)  │
│ Saves cart to browser storage               │
└──────────────┬───────────��──────────────────┘
               ↓
┌──────────────────���──────────────────────────┐
│ Components re-render with new cart          │
│ Cart badge updates count                    │
│ Cart panel shows course                     │
│ Button text: &quot;In cart&quot; (disabled)           │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2 id="-testing-strategy"><strong>🧪 TESTING STRATEGY</strong></h2>
<h3 id="vitest-configuration"><strong>Vitest Configuration</strong></h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vitest.config.js</span>
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Environment</span>: jsdom (simulates browser <span class="hljs-variable constant_">DOM</span>)
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Test</span> <span class="hljs-attr">files</span>: **<span class="hljs-comment">/*.test.jsx, **/</span>*.<span class="hljs-property">spec</span>.<span class="hljs-property">jsx</span>
- <span class="hljs-title class_">Coverage</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Tracking</span> components &amp; hooks

<span class="hljs-comment">// src/App.test.jsx</span>
✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Cart</span> component renders
✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Course</span> cards render
✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Enroll</span> buttons are clickable
✓ <span class="hljs-title class_">Toast</span> notifications appear
✓ <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span> persistence
</code></pre>

<h2 id="-responsive-design"><strong>📱 RESPONSIVE DESIGN</strong></h2>
<h3 id="navbar-responsiveness"><strong>Navbar Responsiveness</strong></h3>
<pre><code>Desktop (&gt;992px):
- Full horizontal menu
- Dropdown hover triggers
- Cart button always visible

Tablet (576-992px):
- Collapsible menu drawer
- Touch-friendly dropdowns
- Cart panel slide-in

Mobile (&lt;576px):
- Hamburger icon opens drawer
- Single-column layout
- Bottom-fixed cart button
- Full-screen cart panel
</code></pre>
<h3 id="course-grid-responsive"><strong>Course Grid Responsive</strong></h3>
<pre><code>Desktop:  4 columns (1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr)
Tablet:   2 columns (1fr 1fr)
Mobile:   1 column  (100%)
</code></pre>

<h2 id="️-build--deployment"><strong>⚙️ BUILD &amp; DEPLOYMENT</strong></h2>
<h3 id="npm-scripts"><strong>npm Scripts</strong></h3>
<pre><code class="language-bash">npm run dev      <span class="hljs-comment"># Start dev server with HMR</span>
npm run build    <span class="hljs-comment"># Build optimized production bundle</span>
npm run preview  <span class="hljs-comment"># Preview production build locally</span>
npm run lint     <span class="hljs-comment"># Run ESLint to check code quality</span>
npm run <span class="hljs-built_in">test</span>     <span class="hljs-comment"># Run Vitest unit tests</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="vite-build-optimization"><strong>Vite Build Optimization</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>Rolldown-Vite</strong>: Ultra-fast bundling</li>
<li><strong>Tree-shaking</strong>: Removes unused code</li>
<li><strong>Code splitting</strong>: Lazy load routes</li>
<li><strong>CSS extraction</strong>: Separate CSS files</li>
<li><strong>Minification</strong>: Reduces bundle size</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="-performance-metrics"><strong>📈 PERFORMANCE METRICS</strong></h2>
<h3 id="optimization-techniques"><strong>Optimization Techniques</strong></h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-number">1.</span> useMemo
   - <span class="hljs-title class_">Prevents</span> unnecessary recalculations
   - <span class="hljs-title class_">Example</span>: cartPricing calculation

<span class="hljs-number">2.</span> useCallback
   - <span class="hljs-title class_">Memoizes</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> references
   - addToCart, removeFromCart don<span class="hljs-string">&#x27;t change

3. Code Splitting
   - React Router lazy loads pages
   - Reduces initial bundle size

4. CSS Optimization
   - CSS Variables reduce duplication
   - Minimal unused styles

5. Image Optimization
   - CDN-hosted SVG icons (devicons)
   - Async decoding attribute
</span></code></pre>
<h3 id="bundle-analysis"><strong>Bundle Analysis</strong></h3>
<ul>
<li>React &amp; React-DOM: ~42KB</li>
<li>React Router: ~15KB</li>
<li>Bootstrap: ~25KB</li>
<li>Other libs: ~20KB</li>
<li><strong>Total gzip: ~70-80KB</strong></li>
</ul>

<h2 id="-learning-outcomes"><strong>🎓 LEARNING OUTCOMES</strong></h2>
<p>By studying this project, you'll understand:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Modern React Architecture</strong> - Component composition, hooks, context</li>
<li><strong>State Management</strong> - Context API without Redux</li>
<li><strong>Performance Optimization</strong> - useMemo, useCallback patterns</li>
<li><strong>Professional Styling</strong> - CSS-in-JS alternatives, design systems</li>
<li><strong>Responsive Design</strong> - Mobile-first approach, breakpoints</li>
<li><strong>Browser APIs</strong> - localStorage, requestAnimationFrame</li>
<li><strong>Testing</strong> - Unit tests with Vitest</li>
<li><strong>Deployment</strong> - GitHub Pages, build optimization</li>
<li><strong>UX/UI Best Practices</strong> - Accessibility, notifications, user feedback</li>
<li><strong>Modern Tooling</strong> - Vite, ESLint, version management</li>
</ol>

<pre><code class="language-markdown"><span class="hljs-section"># 📚 LEARNHUB E-LEARNING PLATFORM</span>

<span class="hljs-section">## Complete Technical Documentation &amp; Analysis</span>

<span class="hljs-section">### From Fundamentals to Advanced Implementation</span>

---

<span class="hljs-section"># TABLE OF CONTENTS</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span> Project Overview &amp; Architecture

<span class="hljs-bullet">8.</span> State Management Deep Dive

<span class="hljs-bullet">10.</span> Testing Strategy
<span class="hljs-bullet">11.</span> Performance Optimization
<span class="hljs-bullet">12.</span> Deployment &amp; Build Process
<span class="hljs-bullet">13.</span> Accessibility &amp; UX
<span class="hljs-bullet">14.</span> Security Considerations
<span class="hljs-bullet">15.</span> Future Enhancements &amp; Scalability

---

<span class="hljs-section"># PART 1: PROJECT OVERVIEW &amp; ARCHITECTURE</span>

<span class="hljs-section">## 1.1 What is LearnHub?</span>

LearnHub is a <span class="hljs-strong">**modern, professional e-learning platform**</span> built with React 19, designed to demonstrate contemporary web development best practices. It&#x27;s a single-page application (SPA) that allows users to:

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Browse a catalog of 44+ courses
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Add courses to a shopping cart
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> View detailed course information
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Persist cart data using browser storage
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Toggle between light and dark themes
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Experience a responsive, mobile-first UI

<span class="hljs-section">## 1.2 Key Statistics</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Repository**</span>: Rohith-180503/LEARNHUB-E-LEARNING-WEBSITE
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Created**</span>: October 20, 2025
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Language Composition**</span>: JavaScript (66%), CSS (33.6%), HTML (0.4%)
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Total Code Size**</span>: ~60-70 KB (production)
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Total Courses**</span>: 44 with categorized content
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Deployment**</span>: GitHub Pages

<span class="hljs-section">## 1.3 Architecture Overview</span>

The application follows a <span class="hljs-strong">**Layered Architecture Pattern**</span>:
</code></pre>
<p>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ PRESENTATION LAYER │
│ Pages (Home, Explore, Resources, Instructors) │
│ Each page displays course content dynamically │
└─────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘
↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ COMPONENT LAYER │
│ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ ┌──────────────┐ │
│ │ Navbar │ │ Cart │ │ Course │ │
│ │ Component │ │ Component │ │ Component │ │
│ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ └──────────────┘ │
└─────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘
↓
┌───────────────────────────────────���─────────────────────┐
│ STATE MANAGEMENT &amp; LOGIC LAYER │
│ CartContext.jsx (Context API) │
│ • Global state for shopping cart │
│ • Methods: addToCart, removeFromCart, clearCart │
│ • localStorage persistence │
└─────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘
↓
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ DATA LAYER │
│ • fakeData.js (44 mock courses) │
│ • localStorage (cart persistence) │
│ • Browser APIs │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘</p>
<pre><code>

# PART 2: TECHNOLOGY STACK DEEP DIVE

## 2.1 Frontend Framework

### React 19.1.1 - The UI Library

**What is React?**
React is a JavaScript library for building user interfaces using reusable components. It uses a &quot;declarative&quot; approach where you describe what the UI should look like, and React handles updating the DOM.

**Why React 19?**
- Latest features and optimizations
- Improved server component support
- Better TypeScript integration
- Enhanced debugging tools
- Performance improvements

**Key React Concepts Used in LearnHub:**

1. **Functional Components**
   - Pure JavaScript functions that return JSX
   - Simpler and more popular than class components
   - Example: `const Course = ({ course }) =&gt; { return (...) }`

2. **JSX (JavaScript XML)**
   - Write HTML-like syntax in JavaScript
   - Gets compiled to `React.createElement()` calls
   - Makes code more readable

3. **Props (Properties)**
   - Way to pass data from parent to child component
   - Read-only, immutable data flow
   - Example: `&lt;Course course={courseData} addToCart={addFn} /&gt;`

4. **Hooks**
   - useState: Manage component-level state
   - useEffect: Handle side effects (data fetching, DOM updates)
   - useContext: Consume global context
   - useCallback: Memoize functions
   - useMemo: Memoize computed values
   - useRef: Access DOM directly
   - useLocation, useNavigate: Router hooks

### React-DOM 19.1.1

Connects React components to the actual DOM:

```javascript
// src/main.jsx
import { createRoot } from 'react-dom/client';

const root = createRoot(document.getElementById('root'));
root.render(&lt;App /&gt;);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="22-routing-react-router-dom-7132">2.2 Routing: React Router DOM 7.13.2</h2>
<p><strong>What is routing?</strong>
Routing allows you to display different pages without full page reloads (SPA behavior).</p>
<p><strong>React Router Features in LearnHub:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// src/App.jsx - Route Configuration</span>
&lt;<span class="hljs-title class_">Routes</span>&gt;
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Home</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/all&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">AllCourses</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/web-development&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">WebDevelopment</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/data-science&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">DataScience</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/cloud-computing&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">CloudComputing</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/ui-ux-design&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">UiUxDesign</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/blog&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Blog</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/community&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Community</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/success-stories&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">SuccessStories</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/documentation&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Documentation</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/instructors&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Instructors</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;</span>
&lt;/<span class="hljs-title class_">Routes</span>&gt;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>How it works:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>BrowserRouter wraps the app (in main.jsx)</li>
<li>Routes matches URL path to component</li>
<li>URL changes without full page reload</li>
<li>Component renders based on matched route</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="23-state-management-react-context-api">2.3 State Management: React Context API</h2>
<p><strong>Why Context API and not Redux?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Redux is overkill for this app's state complexity</li>
<li>Context API is built into React (no external dependency)</li>
<li>Simpler to learn and implement</li>
<li>Perfect for global state like shopping cart</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Context API Flow:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// 1. Create Context</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_">createContext</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// 2. Create Provider Component</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">CartProvider</span>(<span class="hljs-params">{ children }</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>([]);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> value = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(
    <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> ({
      cart,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartCount</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartTotal</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>),
      <span class="hljs-attr">addToCart</span>: <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> {
        <span class="hljs-comment">/* add logic */</span>
      },
      <span class="hljs-attr">removeFromCart</span>: <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">id</span>) =&gt;</span> {
        <span class="hljs-comment">/* remove logic */</span>
      },
      <span class="hljs-attr">clearCart</span>: <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
        <span class="hljs-comment">/* clear logic */</span>
      },
    }),
    [cart],
  );

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span> <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{value}</span>&gt;</span>{children}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span>&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// 3. Create Custom Hook to use Context</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> ctx = <span class="hljs-title function_">useContext</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!ctx) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;useCart must be used within CartProvider&quot;</span>);
  }
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ctx;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// 4. Wrap App with Provider</span>
&lt;<span class="hljs-title class_">CartProvider</span>&gt;
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span></span>
&lt;/<span class="hljs-title class_">CartProvider</span>&gt;;

<span class="hljs-comment">// 5. Use in components</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();
</code></pre>
<h2 id="24-styling-bootstrap-538--custom-css">2.4 Styling: Bootstrap 5.3.8 + Custom CSS</h2>
<h3 id="bootstrap-usage">Bootstrap Usage</h3>
<p>Bootstrap is a CSS framework providing:</p>
<ul>
<li>Pre-built responsive grid system</li>
<li>Utility classes (padding, margin, etc.)</li>
<li>Component styles</li>
<li>Responsive breakpoints</li>
</ul>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// In main.jsx - Import Bootstrap CSS</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;bootstrap/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css&quot;</span>;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Grid System in Bootstrap:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-html"><span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 12-column grid system --&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">class</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;container&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">class</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;row&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">class</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;col-md-8&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Content (8 columns on medium+ screens)<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">class</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;col-md-4&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Sidebar (4 columns on medium+ screens)<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="custom-css-with-css-variables">Custom CSS with CSS Variables</h3>
<p><strong>CSS Variables (Design Tokens):</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* src/styles/index.css */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:root</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Color Palette */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--accent-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#3b82f6</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Primary Blue */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--accent-hover</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#2563eb</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Hover State */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--accent-deep</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#1d4ed8</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Deep Blue */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--accent-violet</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#6366f1</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Secondary Color */</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Semantic Colors */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--danger</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#e11d48</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Error/Delete */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--success</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#0f766e</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Success State */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--success-bright</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#14b8a6</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Bright Success */</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Surfaces &amp; Backgrounds */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--surface-page</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#f8fafc</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Page Background */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--surface-elevated</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#ffffff</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Cards, Modals */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--surface-muted</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#f1f5f9</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Secondary Background */</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Text Colors */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--text-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#1e293b</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Primary Text */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--secondary-text-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#64748b</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Secondary Text */</span>
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Benefits of CSS Variables:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Single source of truth</strong> - Change one variable to update entire theme</li>
<li><strong>Dark mode easy</strong> - Override variables in <code>body.dark-mode</code></li>
<li><strong>Consistency</strong> - All colors follow the design system</li>
<li><strong>Maintainability</strong> - Easy to update brand colors</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>Dark Mode Implementation:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-selector-tag">body</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.dark-mode</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attr">--surface-page</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#0f172a</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Dark background */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--text-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#f8fafc</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Light text */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--accent-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#60a5fa</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Lighter accent */</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* ... override all colors */</span>
}
</code></pre>
<p>Toggle dark mode:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// In Navbar.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [darkMode, setDarkMode] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(
  <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;theme&quot;</span>) === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;dark&quot;</span>,
);

<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">body</span>.<span class="hljs-property">classList</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">toggle</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;dark-mode&quot;</span>, darkMode);
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;theme&quot;</span>, darkMode ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;dark&quot;</span> : <span class="hljs-string">&quot;light&quot;</span>);
}, [darkMode]);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="25-notifications-react-toastify-1105">2.5 Notifications: React Toastify 11.0.5</h2>
<p><strong>What are toasts?</strong>
Non-blocking messages that appear briefly to notify user of actions.</p>
<p><strong>Setup:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// main.jsx - Import Toastify CSS</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify/dist/ReactToastify.css&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// App.jsx - Add ToastContainer</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">ToastContainer</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">position</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;bottom-center&quot;</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">autoClose</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{2800}</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">closeOnClick</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">pauseOnHover</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">role</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;alert&quot;</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">theme</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;colored&quot;</span>
/&gt;</span></span>;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Usage in components:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { toast } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Success toast</span>
toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">`Added to cart: <span class="hljs-subst">${title}</span>`</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Info toast</span>
toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cart cleared&quot;</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Error toast (if needed)</span>
toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Something went wrong!&quot;</span>);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="26-build-tool-vite-rolldown-7114">2.6 Build Tool: Vite (Rolldown) 7.1.14</h2>
<p><strong>What is Vite?</strong>
Modern build tool that provides:</p>
<ul>
<li>Lightning-fast development server (HMR - Hot Module Replacement)</li>
<li>Ultra-fast build process</li>
<li>Code splitting</li>
<li>Optimization</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Vite Config:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vite.config.js</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { defineConfig } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vite&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> react <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@vitejs/plugin-react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">defineConfig</span>({
  <span class="hljs-attr">plugins</span>: [<span class="hljs-title function_">react</span>()], <span class="hljs-comment">// Enable React JSX transformation</span>
});
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Build Process:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>Development: <code>npm run dev</code> → Fast dev server with HMR</li>
<li>Production: <code>npm run build</code> → Optimized bundle in /dist folder</li>
<li>Preview: <code>npm run preview</code> → Test production build locally</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>Why Vite over Webpack?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>10-100x faster development startup</li>
<li>Instant HMR regardless of app size</li>
<li>Optimized build output</li>
<li>Built-in support for modern tools</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="27-testing-vitest-324--react-testing-library-1630">2.7 Testing: Vitest 3.2.4 + React Testing Library 16.3.0</h2>
<p><strong>What is Vitest?</strong>
Fast unit testing framework compatible with Jest but built on Vite.</p>
<p><strong>Configuration:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vitest.config.js</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">defineConfig</span>({
  <span class="hljs-attr">test</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">environment</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;jsdom&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// Simulate browser DOM</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">globals</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// No need to import describe, test, etc.</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">setupFiles</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">&quot;./src/setupTests.js&quot;</span>],
  },
});
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Testing Example:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// src/App.test.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { render, screen } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@testing-library/react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { describe, test, expect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vitest&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">App</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./App.jsx&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-title function_">describe</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Online Learning App&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;renders My Cart heading&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(
      screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByRole</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;heading&quot;</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-regexp">/my cart/i</span> }),
    ).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });

  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;renders at least one course&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByText</span>(<span class="hljs-regexp">/Complete Linux Training/i</span>)).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="28-code-quality-eslint-9360">2.8 Code Quality: ESLint 9.36.0</h2>
<p><strong>What is ESLint?</strong>
Static analysis tool that finds and fixes problems in JavaScript code.</p>
<p><strong>ESLint helps prevent:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Unused variables</li>
<li>Missing semicolons</li>
<li>Incorrect hook usage</li>
<li>Accessibility issues</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h1 id="part-3-project-structure--file-organization">PART 3: PROJECT STRUCTURE &amp; FILE ORGANIZATION</h1>

</code></pre>
<h2 id="32-understanding-file-organization">3.2 Understanding File Organization</h2>
<h3 id="why-this-structure">Why This Structure?</h3>
<p><strong>1. Separation of Concerns</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Each folder has a specific responsibility</li>
<li>Easy to find code by feature or type</li>
<li>Scales well as project grows</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>2. Component Isolation</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Each component has its own folder</li>
<li>Component.jsx + Component.css together</li>
<li>Easy to import and reuse</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>3. State Management Centralization</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>All global state in <code>/context</code></li>
<li>Easy to find and modify</li>
<li>Clear separation from UI components</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>4. Data Layer Separation</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><code>/fakeData</code> contains mock data</li>
<li>Easy to replace with API calls later</li>
<li>Single source of truth for data</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h1 id="part-4-html--entry-points">PART 4: HTML &amp; ENTRY POINTS</h1>
<h2 id="41-indexhtml---the-single-html-file">4.1 index.html - The Single HTML File</h2>
<pre><code class="language-html"><span class="hljs-meta">&lt;!doctype <span class="hljs-keyword">html</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">html</span> <span class="hljs-attr">lang</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;en&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">head</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 1. Character encoding --&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">meta</span> <span class="hljs-attr">charset</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;UTF-8&quot;</span> /&gt;</span>

    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 2. Favicon for browser tab --&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">link</span> <span class="hljs-attr">rel</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;icon&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;image/svg+xml&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">href</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/vite.svg&quot;</span> /&gt;</span>

    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 3. Viewport for responsive design --&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">meta</span> <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;viewport&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">content</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0&quot;</span> /&gt;</span>

    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 4. Page title --&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">title</span>&gt;</span>online-learning-website<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">title</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">head</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">body</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 5. React root element - React renders here --&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;root&quot;</span>&gt;</span><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 6. Main JavaScript entry point (as ES module) --&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">script</span> <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;module&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">src</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/src/main.jsx&quot;</span>&gt;</span><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">script</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">body</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">html</span>&gt;</span>
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Explanation:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li><strong><code>&lt;!doctype html&gt;</code></strong> - Tells browser this is HTML5</li>
<li><strong><code>&lt;meta charset=&quot;UTF-8&quot;&gt;</code></strong> - Supports all characters (emoji, special chars)</li>
<li><strong><code>&lt;meta name=&quot;viewport&quot;&gt;</code></strong> - Makes site responsive on mobile</li>
<li><strong><code>&lt;div id=&quot;root&quot;&gt;</code></strong> - Where React mounts the app</li>
<li><strong><code>&lt;script type=&quot;module&quot;&gt;</code></strong> - Loads main.jsx as ES module (modern JavaScript)</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>Single-Page Application (SPA):</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Only ONE HTML file for entire app</li>
<li>React replaces content dynamically</li>
<li>No page reloads when navigating</li>
<li>Much faster user experience</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="42-mainjsx---react-entry-point">4.2 main.jsx - React Entry Point</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">StrictMode</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { createRoot } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-dom/client&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">App</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./App.jsx&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;bootstrap/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify/dist/ReactToastify.css&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./styles/index.css&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BrowserRouter</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// 1. Create root</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> root = <span class="hljs-title function_">createRoot</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;root&quot;</span>));

<span class="hljs-comment">// 2. Render app with Router and StrictMode</span>
root.<span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">StrictMode</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">BrowserRouter</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">BrowserRouter</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">StrictMode</span>&gt;</span></span>,
);
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Line by Line:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li><strong><code>createRoot()</code></strong> - Create React root to render into</li>
<li><strong><code>StrictMode</code></strong> - Development tool to catch bugs (removed in production)</li>
<li><strong><code>BrowserRouter</code></strong> - Enable client-side routing</li>
<li><strong>CSS Imports</strong> - Load global styles in order:
<ul>
<li>Bootstrap (resets &amp; utilities)</li>
<li>Toast notifications</li>
<li>Custom theme variables</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<hr>

<h2 id="53-navbarcss---complex-navigation-styling-853-lines">5.3 Navbar.css - Complex Navigation Styling (853 lines)</h2>
<h3 id="navigation-bar-structure">Navigation Bar Structure</h3>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-selector-class">.modern-navbar</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attr">--transition-speed</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0.3s</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">position</span>: sticky; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Stick to top during scroll */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">top</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">z-index</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1000</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Above everything except modal overlays */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">100%</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">background</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--nav-bg);

  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Glassmorphism Effect */</span>
  backdrop-<span class="hljs-attribute">filter</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">blur</span>(<span class="hljs-number">14px</span>) <span class="hljs-built_in">saturate</span>(<span class="hljs-number">1.35</span>);

  <span class="hljs-attribute">border-bottom</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1px</span> solid <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--border-subtle);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">box-shadow</span>:
    <span class="hljs-number">0</span> <span class="hljs-number">1px</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">rgba</span>(<span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">255</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.55</span>) inset,

  <span class="hljs-attribute">font-weight</span>: <span class="hljs-number">800</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">letter-spacing</span>: -<span class="hljs-number">0.02em</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">text-transform</span>: none;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-deep);
}

<span class="hljs-selector-tag">body</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.dark-mode</span> <span class="hljs-selector-class">.course-card__price-value</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-hover);
}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="card-button-cta---call-to-action">Card Button (CTA - Call to Action)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-selector-class">.course-card__cta</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">flex</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">min-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">7rem</span>;

<span class="hljs-selector-class">.course-card__cta</span><span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:hover</span><span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:not</span>(<span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:disabled</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">transform</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">translateY</span>(-<span class="hljs-number">1px</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">/* Slight lift */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">filter</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">brightness</span>(<span class="hljs-number">1.05</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">/* Slightly brighter */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">box-shadow</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span> <span class="hljs-number">6px</span> <span class="hljs-number">22px</span> <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-glow);

<span class="hljs-selector-class">.course-card__cta</span><span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:disabled</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">background</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--surface-muted);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--secondary-text-color);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">box-shadow</span>: none;

  <span class="hljs-attribute">filter</span>: none;

  <span class="hljs-attribute">background</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">rgba</span>(<span class="hljs-number">51</span>, <span class="hljs-number">65</span>, <span class="hljs-number">85</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0.6</span>);
