<hr>
<h1 id="part-6-javascriptreact-fundamentals-used">PART 6: JAVASCRIPT/REACT FUNDAMENTALS USED</h1>
<h2 id="61-es6-javascript-features">6.1 ES6+ JavaScript Features</h2>
<h3 id="1-arrow-functions">1. Arrow Functions</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Traditional function</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span>(<span class="hljs-params">a, b</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> a + b;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Arrow function (cleaner)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">a, b</span>) =&gt; a + b;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Arrow function with body</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">a, b</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> result = a + b;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> result;
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// In React components</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleClick</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Clicked!&quot;</span>);
};
</code></pre>
<h3 id="2-destructuring">2. Destructuring</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Object destructuring - extract specific properties</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> course = {
  <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;React Basics&quot;</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">price</span>: <span class="hljs-number">29.99</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">instructor</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;John Doe&quot;</span>,
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// Instead of: const title = course.title;</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { title, price, instructor } = course;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Array destructuring</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> colors = [<span class="hljs-string">&quot;red&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;green&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;blue&quot;</span>];
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [primary, secondary, tertiary] = colors;

<span class="hljs-comment">// In function parameters</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Course</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">{ course, addToCart }</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// course and addToCart are already extracted from props</span>
};
</code></pre>
<h3 id="3-spread-operator">3. Spread Operator</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Copy array</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> original = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>];
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> copy = [...original]; <span class="hljs-comment">// [1, 2, 3]</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Combine arrays</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> arr1 = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>];
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> arr2 = [<span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>];
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> combined = [...arr1, ...arr2]; <span class="hljs-comment">// [1, 2, 3, 4]</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Add to array</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> items = [{ <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span> }];
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> newItems = [...items, { <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2</span> }];

<span class="hljs-comment">// In Cart context - add course without mutating</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([...cart, course]);
</code></pre>
<h3 id="4-template-literals">4. Template Literals</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// String concatenation</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> old = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Hello &quot;</span> + name + <span class="hljs-string">&quot;!&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Template literal with ${}</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> modern = <span class="hljs-string">`Hello <span class="hljs-subst">${name}</span>!`</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Multi-line strings</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> message = <span class="hljs-string">`
  Welcome to LearnHub!
  Price: $<span class="hljs-subst">${price}</span>
`</span>;
</code></pre>
<h3 id="5-ternary-operator">5. Ternary Operator</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// If-else as expression</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> status = isEnrolled ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Enrolled&quot;</span> : <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Not enrolled&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Nested ternary (less readable)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> color =
  status === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;active&quot;</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;green&quot;</span> : status === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;pending&quot;</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;yellow&quot;</span> : <span class="hljs-string">&quot;red&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Better - use if-else for complex logic</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="6-array-methods">6. Array Methods</h3>
<h4 id="map---transform-array">map() - Transform array</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Transform each course into JSX</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> courseElements = courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> (
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course.id}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>
));

<span class="hljs-comment">// Each course becomes a Course component</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="filter---remove-items">filter() - Remove items</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Remove specific item from array</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">removeFromCart</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">id</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">filter</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> !== id));
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// cart.filter() returns new array with items where id !== id</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="reduce---aggregate-data">reduce() - Aggregate data</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Calculate total price</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartTotal = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Starts with sum = 0</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// For each item: sum = sum + item.price</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns final sum</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Example: [10, 20, 30].reduce((sum, n) =&gt; sum + n, 0) = 60</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="some---check-if-any-item-matches">some() - Check if any item matches</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Check if course already in cart</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> isEnrolled = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">some</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns true if ANY item matches condition</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns false if NO items match</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="find---get-first-matching-item">find() - Get first matching item</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Find specific course</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> course = courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">find</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">c</span>) =&gt;</span> c.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns first matching item or undefined</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="7-optional-chaining-">7. Optional Chaining (?.)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Safely access nested properties</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> name = user?.<span class="hljs-property">profile</span>?.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// If user is null/undefined, returns undefined instead of error</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Instead of: user &amp;&amp; user.profile &amp;&amp; user.profile.name</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="8-nullish-coalescing-">8. Nullish Coalescing (??)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Use default value if null or undefined</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> name = user.<span class="hljs-property">name</span> ?? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Guest&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Different from || which treats false/0 as falsy</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// email || &quot;no-email&quot; ��� &quot;no-email&quot; if email is false</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// email ?? &quot;no-email&quot; → &quot;no-email&quot; ONLY if email is null/undefined</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="62-react-hooks-deep-dive">6.2 React Hooks Deep Dive</h2>
<h3 id="usestate---state-management">useState - State Management</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useState } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Course</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Declare state: [currentValue, functionToUpdate]</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [isEnrolled, setIsEnrolled] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// isEnrolled = false initially</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// setIsEnrolled = function to update isEnrolled</span>

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleEnroll</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setIsEnrolled</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">true</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// Update state</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Component re-renders with new state</span>
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span> <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{handleEnroll}</span>&gt;</span>{isEnrolled ? &quot;Enrolled&quot; : &quot;Enroll&quot;}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// Multiple state variables</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>([]);
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [total, setTotal] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [darkMode, setDarkMode] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Key Points:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>setState updates cause component re-render</li>
<li>Use functional updates when new state depends on old state</li>
<li>Never directly mutate state</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="useeffect---side-effects">useEffect - Side Effects</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useEffect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Cart</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>([]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Effect runs AFTER component renders</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Component mounted or dependencies changed&quot;</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Save cart to localStorage</span>
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(cart));

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Optional cleanup function</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Component unmounting or before re-effect&quot;</span>);
    };
  }, [cart]); <span class="hljs-comment">// Dependency array - effect runs when cart changes</span>
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// Effect timing:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - No dependency array: runs after EVERY render</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Empty array []: runs ONCE on mount</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - [cart]: runs when cart changes</span>
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Common Use Cases:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>Fetch data from API</li>
<li>Save to localStorage</li>
<li>Subscribe to events</li>
<li>Clean up resources</li>
</ol>
<h3 id="usecontext---consume-global-state">useContext - Consume Global State</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useContext } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;../context/CartContext&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Product</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Get values from context</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart, removeFromCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useContext</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Can now use cart, addToCart, removeFromCart</span>
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// Better - use custom hook</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();
</code></pre>
<h3 id="usecallback---memoize-functions">useCallback - Memoize Functions</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useCallback } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">CartProvider</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">{ children }</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>([]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Without useCallback - new function created every render</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">addToCart_bad</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([...cart, course]);
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// With useCallback - same function reference if deps unchanged</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> addToCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> [...prev, course]); <span class="hljs-comment">// Use prev to avoid stale closure</span>
  }, []); <span class="hljs-comment">// Empty deps - never changes</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Benefits:</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Function reference stays same</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Prevents unnecessary re-renders of child components</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Improves performance</span>
};
</code></pre>
<h3 id="usememo---memoize-computed-values">useMemo - Memoize Computed Values</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useMemo } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Navbar</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">{ cart }</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Without useMemo - calculated every render</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartPricing_bad = {
    <span class="hljs-attr">subtotal</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>),
    <span class="hljs-attr">discount</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> &gt; <span class="hljs-number">2</span> ? total * <span class="hljs-number">0.1</span> : <span class="hljs-number">0</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">tax</span>: total * <span class="hljs-number">0.05</span>,
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// With useMemo - calculated only when deps change</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartPricing = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> subtotal = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> discount = subtotal &gt;= <span class="hljs-number">100</span> ? subtotal * <span class="hljs-number">0.08</span> : <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> platformFee = cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> ? <span class="hljs-number">2.99</span> : <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> {
      subtotal,
      discount,
      platformFee,
      <span class="hljs-attr">total</span>: <span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">max</span>(subtotal - discount + platformFee, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>),
    };
  }, [cart]); <span class="hljs-comment">// Only recalculate when cart changes</span>

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>Subtotal: ${cartPricing.subtotal}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>Discount: -${cartPricing.discount}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>Total: ${cartPricing.total}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
};
</code></pre>
<h3 id="useref---reference-to-dom-element">useRef - Reference to DOM Element</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useRef } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">CartPanel</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> panelRef = <span class="hljs-title function_">useRef</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleScroll</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access DOM element directly</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (panelRef.<span class="hljs-property">current</span>) {
      panelRef.<span class="hljs-property">current</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">behavior</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span> });
    }
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">ref</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{panelRef}</span>&gt;</span>
      {/* This div can be accessed via panelRef.current */}
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
};
</code></pre>
<h3 id="custom-hooks---usecart">Custom Hooks - useCart</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// src/context/CartContext.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> {
  createContext,
  useContext,
  useState,
  useCallback,
  useMemo,
} <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_">createContext</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">CartProvider</span>(<span class="hljs-params">{ children }</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Lazy initialization - load from localStorage</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> saved = <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> saved ? <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(saved) : [];
  });

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Persist to localStorage whenever cart changes</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(cart));
  }, [cart]);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> addToCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> {
      <span class="hljs-comment">// Check if already in cart</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (prev.<span class="hljs-title function_">some</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>)) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> prev; <span class="hljs-comment">// Don&#x27;t add duplicate</span>
      }
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [...prev, course];
    });
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> removeFromCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">id</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> prev.<span class="hljs-title function_">filter</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> !== id));
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> clearCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([]);
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> value = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(
    <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> ({
      cart,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartCount</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartTotal</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + <span class="hljs-title class_">Number</span>(item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>),
      addToCart,
      removeFromCart,
      clearCart,
    }),
    [cart, addToCart, removeFromCart, clearCart],
  );

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span> <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{value}</span>&gt;</span>{children}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span>&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Custom hook to use cart context</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> ctx = <span class="hljs-title function_">useContext</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!ctx) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;useCart must be used within CartProvider&quot;</span>);
  }
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ctx;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Usage in component</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">MyComponent</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart, removeFromCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Can now use cart state and functions</span>
};
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h1 id="part-7-component-by-component-breakdown">PART 7: COMPONENT-BY-COMPONENT BREAKDOWN</h1>
<h2 id="71-cartcontextjsx---the-brain-of-state-management-80-lines">7.1 CartContext.jsx - The Brain of State Management (80 Lines)</h2>
<p><strong>File Size:</strong> 1.8 KB<br>
<strong>Complexity:</strong> Advanced<br>
<strong>Responsibility:</strong> Global cart state, persistence, and logic</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> {
  createContext,
  useCallback,
  useContext,
  useEffect,
  useMemo,
  useState,
} <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">STORAGE_KEY</span> = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// 1. Create context object</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_">createContext</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// 2. Helper function - Load cart from localStorage</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">loadCartFromStorage</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> raw = <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-variable constant_">STORAGE_KEY</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!raw) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> []; <span class="hljs-comment">// Return empty array if no saved data</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> parsed = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(raw);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Array</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">isArray</span>(parsed) ? parsed : []; <span class="hljs-comment">// Validate it&#x27;s an array</span>
  } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> []; <span class="hljs-comment">// If parsing fails, return empty array</span>
  }
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// 3. Provider component - Wraps entire app</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">CartProvider</span>(<span class="hljs-params">{ children }</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Initialize state from localStorage</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(loadCartFromStorage);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// 4. Effect - Save cart to localStorage whenever it changes</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-variable constant_">STORAGE_KEY</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(cart));
    } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> {
      <span class="hljs-comment">/* Ignore quota exceeded or private mode errors */</span>
    }
  }, [cart]); <span class="hljs-comment">// Run whenever cart changes</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// 5. Memoized function - Add course to cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> addToCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> {
      <span class="hljs-comment">// Check if course already in cart</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (prev.<span class="hljs-title function_">some</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>)) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> prev; <span class="hljs-comment">// Don&#x27;t add duplicate</span>
      }
      <span class="hljs-comment">// Add new course to cart</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [...prev, course];
    });
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// 6. Memoized function - Remove course from cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> removeFromCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">id</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> prev.<span class="hljs-title function_">filter</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> !== id));
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// 7. Memoized function - Clear entire cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> clearCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([]);
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// 8. Memoized value object - Contains all context data</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> value = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartTotal = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + <span class="hljs-title class_">Number</span>(item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> {
      cart, <span class="hljs-comment">// Array of course objects</span>
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartCount</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// Number of courses</span>
      cartTotal, <span class="hljs-comment">// Total price</span>
      addToCart, <span class="hljs-comment">// Function to add</span>
      removeFromCart, <span class="hljs-comment">// Function to remove</span>
      clearCart, <span class="hljs-comment">// Function to clear all</span>
    };
  }, [cart, addToCart, removeFromCart, clearCart]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// 9. Provide context to children</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span> <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{value}</span>&gt;</span>{children}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span>&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// 10. Custom hook - Use cart context in components</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> ctx = <span class="hljs-title function_">useContext</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!ctx) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;useCart must be used within a CartProvider&quot;</span>);
  }
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ctx;
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Key Design Patterns:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Lazy Initialization</strong> - Load data only once from localStorage</li>
<li><strong>Memoization</strong> - Functions &amp; values don't change unless dependencies change</li>
<li><strong>Error Handling</strong> - Gracefully handle localStorage errors</li>
<li><strong>Custom Hook</strong> - Convenient way to access context</li>
<li><strong>Validation</strong> - Check for duplicates before adding</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="72-coursejsx---individual-course-card-49-lines">7.2 Course.jsx - Individual Course Card (49 Lines)</h2>
<p><strong>File Size:</strong> 1.5 KB<br>
<strong>Complexity:</strong> Simple<br>
<strong>Responsibility:</strong> Display single course and handle enrollment</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { toast } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useCart } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;../../context/CartContext&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./Course.css&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Component - Receives course data as prop</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Course</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">{ course }</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Destructure course properties</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { title, instructor, price, img } = course;

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Get cart context functions</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Check if already in cart using array.some()</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// some() returns true if ANY element matches condition</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> isEnrolled = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">some</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Format price to 2 decimal places</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> priceLabel =
    <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> price === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;number&quot;</span> ? price.<span class="hljs-title function_">toFixed</span>(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>) : <span class="hljs-title class_">String</span>(price);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Handle enrollment button click</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleEnroll</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (isEnrolled) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// Don&#x27;t add if already enrolled</span>
    <span class="hljs-title function_">addToCart</span>(course);
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">`Added to cart: <span class="hljs-subst">${title}</span>`</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// Show notification</span>
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Semantic HTML - article tag for content</span>
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">article</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
      {/* Image section */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__media&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">img</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__img&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">src</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{img}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">alt</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;&quot;</span> /&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

      {/* Content section */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__body&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        {/* Title */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">h3</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__title&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{title}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">h3</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Instructor info */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__instructor&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          Instructor
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__instructor-name&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{instructor}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Footer - Price and button */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__footer&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          {/* Price */}
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__price&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
            Price
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__price-value&quot;</span>&gt;</span>${priceLabel}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>

          {/* Enroll button */}
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__cta&quot;</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{handleEnroll}</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">disabled</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{isEnrolled}</span> // <span class="hljs-attr">Disabled</span> <span class="hljs-attr">if</span> <span class="hljs-attr">already</span> <span class="hljs-attr">enrolled</span>
          &gt;</span>
            {isEnrolled ? &quot;In cart&quot; : &quot;Add to cart&quot;}
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
};

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Course</span>;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Props:</strong> <code>course</code> object</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>: number,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: string,
  <span class="hljs-attr">instructor</span>: string,
  <span class="hljs-attr">price</span>: number,
  <span class="hljs-attr">img</span>: string (<span class="hljs-variable constant_">URL</span>)
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>State:</strong> None (uses context)</p>
<p><strong>Renders:</strong> Single course card with button</p>
<h2 id="73-cartjsx---shopping-cart-display-132-lines">7.3 Cart.jsx - Shopping Cart Display (132 Lines)</h2>
<p><strong>File Size:</strong> 4.1 KB<br>
<strong>Complexity:</strong> Medium<br>
<strong>Responsibility:</strong> Display cart contents, handle removals, show total</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useEffect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">Link</span>, useLocation, useNavigate } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { toast } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useCart } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;../../context/CartContext&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./Cart.css&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">CART_ANCHOR</span> = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;learning-cart&quot;</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// ID for scroll target</span>

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Cart</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Get cart context values</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, cartTotal, removeFromCart, clearCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Router hooks</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> location = <span class="hljs-title function_">useLocation</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// Current route info</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> navigate = <span class="hljs-title function_">useNavigate</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// Navigate to route</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Effect - Scroll to cart if URL contains #learning-cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (location.<span class="hljs-property">hash</span> !== <span class="hljs-string">`#<span class="hljs-subst">${CART_ANCHOR}</span>`</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> el = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-variable constant_">CART_ANCHOR</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!el) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Use requestAnimationFrame for smooth scrolling</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> t = <span class="hljs-title function_">requestAnimationFrame</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
      el.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">behavior</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">block</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;start&quot;</span> });
    });

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Cleanup</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">cancelAnimationFrame</span>(t);
  }, [location.<span class="hljs-property">pathname</span>, location.<span class="hljs-property">hash</span>]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Handle clear cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleClear</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Show confirmation dialog</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (
      <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span> !== <span class="hljs-string">&quot;undefined&quot;</span> &amp;&amp;
      !<span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">confirm</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Remove all courses from your cart?&quot;</span>)
    ) {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
    }

    <span class="hljs-title function_">clearCart</span>();
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cart cleared&quot;</span>);
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Handle remove single item</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleRemoveOne</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">removeFromCart</span>(course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>);
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">`Removed &quot;<span class="hljs-subst">${course.title}</span>&quot; from cart`</span>);
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">section</span>
      <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{CART_ANCHOR}</span>
      <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;horizontal-cart&quot;</span>
      <span class="hljs-attr">aria-labelledby</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-heading&quot;</span>
    &gt;</span>
      {/* Left side - Cart title and items */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-left&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        {/* Header */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-heading-row&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">h2</span> <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-heading&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-title&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-hidden</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;true&quot;</span>&gt;</span>🛒<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span> My cart
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">h2</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-count-pill&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-live</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;polite&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
            {cart.length === 0
              ? &quot;0 courses&quot;
              : `${cart.length} course${cart.length === 1 ? &quot;&quot; : &quot;s&quot;}`}
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Items list or empty state */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-items-container&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          {cart.length === 0 ? (
            // Empty cart
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-empty-block&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-empty&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Your cart is empty.<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Link</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-empty-cta&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">to</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                Browse courses
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">Link</span>&gt;</span>
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
          ) : (
            // Cart items
            cart.map((course) =&gt; (
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course.id}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip course-chip--rich&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip__text&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip__title&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{course.title}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip__meta&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                    {course.instructor} · ${Number(course.price).toFixed(2)}
                  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
                  <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;remove-btn&quot;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{()</span> =&gt;</span> handleRemoveOne(course)}
                  title=&quot;Remove from cart&quot;
                  aria-label={`Remove ${course.title} from cart`}
                &gt;
                  ✕
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
            ))
          )}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

      {/* Right side - Summary and actions */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-right&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        {/* Total price */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-right-summary&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-total-label&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Estimated total<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-total-price&quot;</span>&gt;</span>${cartTotal.toFixed(2)}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Action buttons */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-actions&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          {cart.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; (
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;&gt;</span>
              {/* Clear cart button */}
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-btn-secondary&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{handleClear}</span>
              &gt;</span>
                Clear cart
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>

              {/* Checkout button (disabled in demo) */}
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-btn-checkout&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">disabled</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Checkout not available in demo&quot;</span>
              &gt;</span>
                Checkout
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/&gt;</span>
          )}

          {/* Back to catalog button (shown if not on home page) */}
          {location.pathname !== &quot;/&quot; &amp;&amp; (
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
              <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
              <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-btn-text&quot;</span>
              <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{()</span> =&gt;</span> navigate({ pathname: &quot;/&quot;, hash: CART_ANCHOR })}
            &gt;
              Back to catalog
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
          )}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
    &lt;/section&gt;
  );
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Features:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Empty state handling</li>
<li>Smooth scroll to cart</li>
<li>Confirmation dialog for clear</li>
<li>Toast notifications</li>
<li>Conditional button display</li>
<li>Accessibility attributes</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="74-navbarjsx---navigation-component-516-lines">7.4 Navbar.jsx - Navigation Component (516 Lines)</h2>
<p><strong>File Size:</strong> 18.6 KB<br>
<strong>Complexity:</strong> Advanced<br>
<strong>Responsibility:</strong> Main navigation, dropdowns, cart panel, theme toggle, mobile menu</p>
<p>This is the most complex component. Let me break it into sections:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useState, useEffect, useRef, useMemo } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

  <span class="hljs-comment">// ... more links</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [activeDropdown, setActiveDropdown] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// Which dropdown active</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cartPanelOpen, setCartPanelOpen] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// Cart panel open</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [darkMode, setDarkMode] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(
    <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span> !== <span class="hljs-string">&quot;undefined&quot;</span> &amp;&amp; <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;theme&quot;</span>) === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;dark&quot;</span>,

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> drawerRef = <span class="hljs-title function_">useRef</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartPanelRef = <span class="hljs-title function_">useRef</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// HOOKS</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// ──���──────────────────</span>

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> location = <span class="hljs-title function_">useLocation</span>();
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> navigate = <span class="hljs-title function_">useNavigate</span>();
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, cartCount, cartTotal, removeFromCart, clearCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();

  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// COMPUTED VALUES</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Memoized price calculations</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartPricing = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> subtotal = <span class="hljs-title class_">Number</span>(cartTotal);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> discount = subtotal &gt;= <span class="hljs-number">100</span> ? subtotal * <span class="hljs-number">0.08</span> : <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 8% off if &gt;= $100</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> platformFee = cartCount &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> ? <span class="hljs-number">2.99</span> : <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> totalPayable = <span class="hljs-title class_">Math</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">max</span>(subtotal - discount + platformFee, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> { subtotal, discount, platformFee, totalPayable };
  }, [cartCount, cartTotal]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// EVENT HANDLERS</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>

      <span class="hljs-attr">block</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;start&quot;</span>,
    });
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">goToMainCart</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCartPanelOpen</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (location.<span class="hljs-property">pathname</span> === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>) {
      <span class="hljs-title function_">scrollToMainCart</span>();
    } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
      <span class="hljs-title function_">navigate</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">pathname</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">hash</span>: <span class="hljs-variable constant_">CART_ANCHOR</span> });
    }
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleNavbarRemove</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">removeFromCart</span>(item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>);
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">`Removed &quot;<span class="hljs-subst">${item.title}</span>&quot; from cart`</span>);
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleNavbarClear</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (cartCount === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (
      <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span> !== <span class="hljs-string">&quot;undefined&quot;</span> &amp;&amp;
      !<span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">confirm</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Remove all courses from your cart?&quot;</span>)
    ) {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
    }
    <span class="hljs-title function_">clearCart</span>();
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCartPanelOpen</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cart cleared&quot;</span>);
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handlePlaceOrder</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (cartCount === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Order review started. Payment integration coming soon.&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCartPanelOpen</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// EFFECTS</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// ─────────────────────</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Close menus on route change</span>

  }, [darkMode]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Close menus on Escape key</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onKey</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">e</span>) =&gt; {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (e.<span class="hljs-property">key</span> === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Escape&quot;</span>) {
        <span class="hljs-title function_">setMobileOpen</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);
        <span class="hljs-title function_">setActiveDropdown</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);
        <span class="hljs-title function_">setCartPanelOpen</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);
      }
    };
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;keydown&quot;</span>, onKey);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">removeEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;keydown&quot;</span>, onKey);
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Close dropdowns on outside click</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handler</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">e</span>) =&gt; {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> t = e.<span class="hljs-property">target</span>;
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (navRef.<span class="hljs-property">current</span>?.<span class="hljs-title function_">contains</span>(t)) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (drawerRef.<span class="hljs-property">current</span>?.<span class="hljs-title function_">contains</span>(t)) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (cartPanelRef.<span class="hljs-property">current</span>?.<span class="hljs-title function_">contains</span>(t)) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;

      <span class="hljs-title function_">setMobileOpen</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);
    };

</code></pre>
<p><strong>Key Features:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Desktop &amp; mobile responsive</li>
<li>Keyboard navigation (Escape key)</li>
<li>Click-outside detection</li>
<li>Smooth animations</li>
<li>Accessibility (ARIA labels)</li>
<li>Price calculations with discounts</li>
<li>Theme toggle with persistence</li>
<li>Toast notifications</li>
</ul>
<hr>

        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/all&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">AllCourses</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/web-development&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">WebDevelopment</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/data-science&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">DataScience</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/cloud-computing&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">CloudComputing</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/ui-ux-design&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">UiUxDesign</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/blog&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Blog</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/community&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Community</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/success-stories&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">SuccessStories</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/documentation&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Documentation</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/instructors&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Instructors</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">Routes</span>&gt;</span>

      {/* Toast notifications container */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">ToastContainer</span>
        <span class="hljs-attr">position</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;bottom-center&quot;</span>
        <span class="hljs-attr">autoClose</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{2800}</span> /* <span class="hljs-attr">2.8</span> <span class="hljs-attr">seconds</span> */
        <span class="hljs-attr">closeOnClick</span>
        <span class="hljs-attr">pauseOnHover</span>
        <span class="hljs-attr">role</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;alert&quot;</span>
        <span class="hljs-attr">theme</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;colored&quot;</span>
      /&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Main App component</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">App</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Wrap everything in CartProvider for global state access</span>
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartProvider</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">AppShell</span> /&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">CartProvider</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">App</span>;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Purpose:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>Define all routes</li>
<li>Provide global context (CartProvider)</li>
<li>Render main layout (Navbar, Cart, Routes)</li>
<li>Configure toast notifications</li>
</ol>

<h1 id="part-9-mainjsx---entry-point-16-lines">PART 9: MAIN.JSX - ENTRY POINT (16 Lines)</h1>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">StrictMode</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { createRoot } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-dom/client&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">App</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./App.jsx&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;bootstrap/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css&quot;</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// Bootstrap styles</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify/dist/ReactToastify.css&quot;</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// Toast styles</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./styles/index.css&quot;</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// Custom global styles</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BrowserRouter</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// 1. Create React root into DOM</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> root = <span class="hljs-title function_">createRoot</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;root&quot;</span>));

<span class="hljs-comment">// 2. Render app with necessary providers</span>
root.<span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">StrictMode</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">BrowserRouter</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">BrowserRouter</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">StrictMode</span>&gt;</span></span>,
);
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Import Order Matters:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li>React libraries</li>
<li>Third-party CSS (Bootstrap, Toastify)</li>
<li>Custom CSS (overrides third-party)</li>
<li>Wrap with providers (Router, App)</li>
</ol>

<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vitest.config.js</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { defineConfig } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vitest/config&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> react <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@vitejs/plugin-react&quot;</span>;
