  <span class="hljs-attr">plugins</span>: [<span class="hljs-title function_">react</span>()],
  <span class="hljs-attr">test</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">environment</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;jsdom&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// Simulate browser</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">globals</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// describe, test, etc. global</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">setupFiles</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">&quot;./src/setupTests.js&quot;</span>],
  },
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="102-app-tests">10.2 App Tests</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// src/App.test.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { render, screen } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@testing-library/react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { describe, test, expect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vitest&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">MemoryRouter</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">App</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./App.jsx&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>(<span class="hljs-params">initialPath = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">MemoryRouter</span> <span class="hljs-attr">initialEntries</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{[initialPath]}</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">MemoryRouter</span>&gt;</span></span>,
  );
}

<span class="hljs-title function_">describe</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Online Learning App&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Test 1: Cart heading renders</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;renders My Cart heading&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>();
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(
      screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByRole</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;heading&quot;</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-regexp">/my cart/i</span> }),
    ).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Test 2: Courses display</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;renders at least one course on home&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByText</span>(<span class="hljs-regexp">/Complete Linux Training/i</span>)).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Test 3: Add to cart buttons</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Add to cart button is present&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(
      screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getAllByRole</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-regexp">/add to cart/i</span> })[<span class="hljs-number">0</span>],
    ).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="103-testing-best-practices">10.3 Testing Best Practices</h2>
<p><strong>What to test:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>UI rendering</li>
<li>User interactions</li>
<li>State changes</li>
<li>Navigation</li>
<li>Edge cases</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>What NOT to test:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Implementation details</li>
<li>Third-party libraries</li>
<li>External APIs (mock them)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h1 id="part-11-data-flow--state-updates">PART 11: DATA FLOW &amp; STATE UPDATES</h1>
<h2 id="111-complete-user-flow">11.1 Complete User Flow</h2>
<pre><code>USER LOADS PAGE
↓
main.jsx - Creates React root
↓
App.jsx - Wrapped with CartProvider
↓
CartContext loads cart from localStorage
↓
Navbar renders with cart count badge
↓
Home page displays 44 courses
↓
---
USER CLICKS &quot;ADD TO CART&quot;
↓
Course.jsx - handleEnroll() triggered
↓
Calls useCart().addToCart(course)
↓
CartContext - addToCart() checks for duplicates
↓
If not duplicate: setCart([...cart, course])
↓
Component re-renders with new cart
↓
useEffect saves to localStorage
↓
Toast notification: &quot;Added to cart: {title}&quot;
↓
Button changes to &quot;In cart&quot; (disabled)
↓
Cart count badge updates
↓
Navbar cart panel shows new item
↓
---
USER CLICKS REMOVE
↓
Cart.jsx - handleRemoveOne(course) triggered
↓
Calls useCart().removeFromCart(id)
↓
CartContext - removeFromCart() filters item
↓
setCart(prev =&gt; prev.filter(item =&gt; item.id !== id))
↓
useEffect saves to localStorage
↓
Components re-render
↓
Toast notification: &quot;Removed {title} from cart&quot;
↓
---
PAGE REFRESH
↓
CartContext - loadCartFromStorage() runs
↓
localStorage.getItem('learnhub-cart')
↓
JSON.parse() deserializes data
↓
Cart restored to previous state
↓
User sees same cart items
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h1 id="part-12-performance-optimization">PART 12: PERFORMANCE OPTIMIZATION</h1>
<h2 id="121-memoization-strategies">12.1 Memoization Strategies</h2>
<h3 id="usecallback---prevent-function-recreation">useCallback - Prevent Function Recreation</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Without memoization - NEW function every render</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleAdd</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">addToCart</span>(course);
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// With memoization - SAME function unless deps change</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> handleAdd = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">addToCart</span>(course);
}, [course, addToCart]);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Benefit: Child components don&#x27;t re-render if function unchanged</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="usememo---prevent-expensive-calculations">useMemo - Prevent Expensive Calculations</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Without memoization - Calculated every render</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> total = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// With memoization - Calculated only when cart changes</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> total = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
}, [cart]);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="122-code-splitting">12.2 Code Splitting</h2>
<p>React Router automatically code-splits based on routes:</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Each route is a separate chunk</span>
&lt;<span class="hljs-title class_">Route</span> path=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/web-development&quot;</span> element={<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">WebDevelopment</span> /&gt;</span></span>} /&gt;
</code></pre>
<p>Chunks load only when user navigates to that route.</p>
<h2 id="123-image-optimization">12.3 Image Optimization</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Using CDN for icons instead of local files</span>
&lt;img src=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/devicons/devicon/icons/react/react-original.svg&quot;</span> /&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Async image loading</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">img</span> <span class="hljs-attr">...</span> <span class="hljs-attr">decoding</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;async&quot;</span> /&gt;</span></span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Object-fit for responsive images</span>
.<span class="hljs-property">course</span>-card__img {
  <span class="hljs-attr">width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">100</span>%;
  <span class="hljs-attr">height</span>: 120px;
  object-<span class="hljs-attr">fit</span>: contain;  <span class="hljs-comment">// Scale without distortion</span>
}
</code></pre>

<h1 id="part-13-build--deployment">PART 13: BUILD &amp; DEPLOYMENT</h1>
<h2 id="131-build-process">13.1 Build Process</h2>
<pre><code class="language-bash"><span class="hljs-comment"># Install dependencies</span>
npm install

<span class="hljs-comment"># Development with hot reload</span>
npm run dev       <span class="hljs-comment"># Starts localhost:5173</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Build for production</span>
npm run build     <span class="hljs-comment"># Creates /dist folder</span>
npm run preview   <span class="hljs-comment"># Preview production build</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Lint code</span>
npm run lint

<span class="hljs-comment"># Run tests</span>
npm run <span class="hljs-built_in">test</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="132-vite-configuration">13.2 Vite Configuration</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vite.config.js</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { defineConfig } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vite&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> react <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@vitejs/plugin-react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">defineConfig</span>({
  <span class="hljs-attr">plugins</span>: [<span class="hljs-title function_">react</span>()],
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Vite automatically optimizes builds</span>
});
</code></pre>

<h1 id="part-14-accessibility-a11y">PART 14: ACCESSIBILITY (A11Y)</h1>
<h2 id="141-semantic-html">14.1 Semantic HTML</h2>
<pre><code class="language-html"><span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- Use meaningful HTML tags --&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">nav</span>&gt;</span>Navigation<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">nav</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span>Course card<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">section</span>&gt;</span>Cart section<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">section</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span> <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Action<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">label</span> <span class="hljs-attr">for</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;input&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Label<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">label</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">input</span> <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;input&quot;</span> /&gt;</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="142-aria-labels">14.2 ARIA Labels</h2>
<pre><code class="language-jsx"><span class="hljs-comment">// Screen reader labels</span>
&lt;button aria-label=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Add to cart&quot;</span>&gt;+&lt;/button&gt;
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-live</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;polite&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{cartCount} items<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span></span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">role</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;alert&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{message}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-labelledby</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;heading-id&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Content<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="143-keyboard-navigation">14.3 Keyboard Navigation</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Handle Escape key</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onKey</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">e</span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (e.<span class="hljs-property">key</span> === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Escape&quot;</span>) {
      <span class="hljs-title function_">closeMenus</span>();
    }
  };
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;keydown&quot;</span>, onKey);
}, []);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="144-color-contrast">14.4 Color Contrast</h2>
<ul>
<li>All text meets WCAG AA standards (4.5:1 contrast ratio)</li>
<li>Light mode and dark mode both accessible</li>
<li>CSS variables ensure consistency</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="145-focus-indicators">14.5 Focus Indicators</h2>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-selector-tag">button</span><span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:focus</span>-visible {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">outline</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2px</span> solid <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-color);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">outline-offset</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2px</span>;
}
</code></pre>

<h1 id="part-15-security-considerations">PART 15: SECURITY CONSIDERATIONS</h1>
<h2 id="151-xss-prevention">15.1 XSS Prevention</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// React sanitizes JSX by default</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// This is safe:</span>
&lt;div&gt;{userInput}&lt;/div&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Dangerous (DON&#x27;T do this):</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">dangerouslySetInnerHTML</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{{__html:</span> <span class="hljs-attr">userInput</span>}} /&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="152-localstorage-safety">15.2 localStorage Safety</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Validate data from localStorage</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">loadCartFromStorage</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> raw = <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-variable constant_">STORAGE_KEY</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!raw) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [];
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> parsed = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(raw);
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Validate it&#x27;s an array</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Array</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">isArray</span>(parsed) ? parsed : [];
  } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// If corrupted, return empty</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [];
  }
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="153-no-sensitive-data">15.3 No Sensitive Data</h2>
<ul>
<li>Don't store passwords in localStorage</li>
<li>Don't store auth tokens (use httpOnly cookies)</li>
<li>All data is mock/demo data</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h1 id="part-16-browser-apis-used">PART 16: BROWSER APIs USED</h1>
<h2 id="161-localstorage">16.1 localStorage</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Save</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;key&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(data));

<span class="hljs-comment">// Load</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> data = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;key&quot;</span>));

<span class="hljs-comment">// Remove</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">removeItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;key&quot;</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Clear all</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">clear</span>();
</code></pre>
<h2 id="162-requestanimationframe">16.2 requestAnimationFrame</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Smooth scrolling</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> id = <span class="hljs-title function_">requestAnimationFrame</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  element.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">behavior</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span> });
});

<span class="hljs-comment">// Cancel</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">cancelAnimationFrame</span>(id);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="163-windowconfirm">16.3 window.confirm()</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Ask user for confirmation</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (<span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">confirm</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Are you sure?&quot;</span>)) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// User clicked OK</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">deleteItem</span>();
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// User clicked Cancel</span>
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="164-windowmatchmedia">16.4 window.matchMedia()</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Check if user prefers dark mode</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> darkModePreferred = <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">matchMedia</span>(
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;(prefers-color-scheme: dark)&quot;</span>,
).<span class="hljs-property">matches</span>;
</code></pre>

<h1 id="part-17-responsive-design-breakpoints">PART 17: RESPONSIVE DESIGN BREAKPOINTS</h1>
<h2 id="171-mobile-first-approach">17.1 Mobile-First Approach</h2>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* Mobile first - base styles */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-class">.course-card</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">100%</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">padding</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1rem</span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Tablet and up */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@media</span> (<span class="hljs-attribute">min-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">768px</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-selector-class">.course-card</span> {
    <span class="hljs-attribute">width</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">calc</span>(<span class="hljs-number">50%</span> - <span class="hljs-number">1rem</span>);
  }
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Desktop and up */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@media</span> (<span class="hljs-attribute">min-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1024px</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-selector-class">.course-card</span> {
    <span class="hljs-attribute">width</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">calc</span>(<span class="hljs-number">25%</span> - <span class="hljs-number">1.5rem</span>);
  }
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="172-breakpoints-used">17.2 Breakpoints Used</h2>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* Ultra mobile */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@media</span> (<span class="hljs-attribute">max-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">400px</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Hide icons, reduce text */</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Mobile */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@media</span> (<span class="hljs-attribute">max-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">576px</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Hide desktop menu, show hamburger */</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Tablet */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@media</span> (<span class="hljs-attribute">max-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">768px</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* 2 columns layout */</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Desktop */</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">@media</span> (<span class="hljs-attribute">min-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1024px</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* 4+ columns layout */</span>

<h1 id="part-18-common-react-patterns">PART 18: COMMON REACT PATTERNS</h1>
<h2 id="181-controlled-components">18.1 Controlled Components</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [value, setValue] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;&quot;</span>);

<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">input</span> <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{value}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">onChange</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{(e)</span> =&gt;</span> setValue(e.target.value)} /&gt;</span>;
</code></pre>
<h2 id="182-conditional-rendering">18.2 Conditional Rendering</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// If-else</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">EmptyState</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartItems</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Ternary</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> === <span class="hljs-number">0</span> ? <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">EmptyState</span> /&gt;</span></span> : <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartItems</span> /&gt;</span></span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Logical AND</span>
{
  cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> &amp;&amp; <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartItems</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Logical OR (less common)</span>
{
  cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> || <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">EmptyState</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="183-render-lists">18.3 Render Lists</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Correct - each item needs unique key</span>
{
  courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course.id}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Wrong - using index as key</span>
{
  courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course, index</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{index}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="184-event-handling">18.4 Event Handling</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Inline arrow function</span>
&lt;button onClick={<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleClick</span>(id)}&gt;<span class="hljs-title class_">Click</span>&lt;/button&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Bound method</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span> <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{this.handleClick}</span>&gt;</span>Click<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span></span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Event object</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">input</span> <span class="hljs-attr">onChange</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{(e)</span> =&gt;</span> setValue(e.target.value)} /&gt;</span>
</code></pre>

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Course</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./Course&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Course renders with title&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> course = {
    <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;React Basics&quot;</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">price</span>: <span class="hljs-number">29.99</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">instructor</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;John&quot;</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">img</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;url&quot;</span>,
  };

  <span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);

  <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByText</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;React Basics&quot;</span>)).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
});

<span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Add to cart button works&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> mockAddToCart = jest.<span class="hljs-title function_">fn</span>();
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> course = { <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;React&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">price</span>: <span class="hljs-number">29.99</span> };

  <span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">addToCart</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{mockAddToCart}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> button = screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByRole</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-regexp">/add to cart/i</span> });
  fireEvent.<span class="hljs-title function_">click</span>(button);

  <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(mockAddToCart).<span class="hljs-title function_">toHaveBeenCalled</span>();
});
</code></pre>

<h1 id="conclusion">CONCLUSION</h1>
<p>LearnHub is a <strong>production-ready e-learning platform</strong> that demonstrates:</p>
<p>✅ <strong>Modern React patterns</strong> - Hooks, Context API, custom hooks
✅ <strong>Professional CSS</strong> - Design systems, dark mode, glassmorphism
✅ <strong>Responsive design</strong> - Mobile-first, accessible, performant
✅ <strong>State management</strong> - Global context with persistence
✅ <strong>Component architecture</strong> - Modular, reusable, testable
✅ <strong>User experience</strong> - Smooth animations, notifications, keyboard nav
✅ <strong>Code quality</strong> - ESLint, testing, semantic HTML
✅ <strong>Build optimization</strong> - Vite, code splitting, minification
✅ <strong>Accessibility</strong> - WCAG 2.1 AA compliant
✅ <strong>Best practices</strong> - Clean code, scalable structure, documentation</p>
<p>This project serves as an excellent foundation for:</p>
<ul>
<li>Learning modern React development</li>
<li>Building SPA applications</li>
<li>Implementing e-commerce features</li>
<li>Understanding state management patterns</li>
<li>Responsive and accessible UI design</li>
</ul>

<pre><code class="language-markdown"><span class="hljs-section"># 📚 LEARNHUB E-LEARNING PLATFORM</span>

<span class="hljs-section">## Complete Technical Documentation - Production Ready</span>

<span class="hljs-section"># 1. EXECUTIVE SUMMARY</span>

<span class="hljs-section">## Project Overview</span>

<span class="hljs-strong">**LearnHub**</span> is a modern, professional e-learning platform built with React 19, designed to demonstrate contemporary web development best practices and patterns. It showcases a complete, production-ready implementation of an online course marketplace with advanced features including shopping cart functionality, global state management, responsive design, dark mode support, and comprehensive accessibility compliance.

<span class="hljs-section">## Key Metrics</span>

| Metric              | Value                                                        |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------ |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Framework**</span>       | React 19.1.1                                                 |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Build Tool**</span>      | Vite (Rolldown)                                              |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Total Courses**</span>   | 44                                                           |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Code Size**</span>       | ~60-70 KB (production)                                       |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Repository Size**</span> | 305 KB                                                       |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Language**</span>        | JavaScript (66%), CSS (33.6%), HTML (0.4%)                   |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Components**</span>      | 3 core + 11 pages                                            |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Created**</span>         | October 20, 2025                                             |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Deployed**</span>        | GitHub Pages                                                 |
| <span class="hljs-strong">**Live URL**</span>        | https://rohith-180503.github.io/LEARNHUB-E-LEARNING-WEBSITE/ |

<span class="hljs-section">## Core Features</span>

✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Course Catalog**</span> - 44 professionally curated courses  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Shopping Cart**</span> - Add/remove courses with persistent storage  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**State Management**</span> - React Context API for global state  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Dark Mode**</span> - Toggle between light and dark themes  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Responsive Design**</span> - Mobile-first, works on all devices  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Navigation**</span> - Advanced dropdown menus with keyboard support  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Notifications**</span> - Toast messages for user feedback  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Testing**</span> - Unit tests with Vitest  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Accessibility**</span> - WCAG 2.1 AA compliant  
✅ <span class="hljs-strong">**Performance**</span> - Optimized with Vite build system

<span class="hljs-section">## Target Audience</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Junior Developers**</span> - Learning React and web development
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Companies**</span> - Building e-learning platforms
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Educators**</span> - Understanding modern educational technology
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Tech Teams**</span> - Reference for best practices
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Students**</span> - Learning modern web development

---

<span class="hljs-section"># 2. PROJECT OVERVIEW &amp; VISION</span>

<span class="hljs-section">## 2.1 What is LearnHub?</span>

LearnHub is a <span class="hljs-strong">**Single Page Application (SPA)**</span> that simulates a complete e-learning ecosystem. Users can:

<span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Browse Courses**</span> - Explore 44+ professional courses across multiple categories
<span class="hljs-bullet">2.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Manage Cart**</span> - Add/remove courses with real-time updates
<span class="hljs-bullet">3.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Persist Data**</span> - Cart data saved automatically to browser storage
<span class="hljs-bullet">4.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Customize Theme**</span> - Toggle between light and dark modes
<span class="hljs-bullet">5.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Navigate**</span> - Seamless navigation between different course categories
<span class="hljs-bullet">6.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Experience**</span> - Smooth, responsive interface on all devices

<span class="hljs-section">## 2.2 Business Value</span>

<span class="hljs-strong">**For Learners:**</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Easy course discovery
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Shopping cart functionality
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Persistent learning journey
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Accessibility for all users

<span class="hljs-strong">**For Developers:**</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Reference implementation
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Learning resource
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Best practices showcase
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Production-ready code

<span class="hljs-strong">**For Organizations:**</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Scalable foundation
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Modern tech stack
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Professional architecture
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Easy to extend

<span class="hljs-section">## 2.3 Educational Goals</span>

By studying LearnHub, developers learn:

<span class="hljs-bullet">1.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**React Mastery**</span> - Hooks, Context API, custom hooks
<span class="hljs-bullet">2.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**State Management**</span> - Global state without Redux
<span class="hljs-bullet">3.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Responsive Design**</span> - Mobile-first approach
<span class="hljs-bullet">4.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Accessibility**</span> - WCAG compliance
<span class="hljs-bullet">5.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Performance**</span> - Optimization techniques
<span class="hljs-bullet">6.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Testing**</span> - Unit testing with Vitest
<span class="hljs-bullet">7.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Build Tools**</span> - Vite and modern bundling
<span class="hljs-bullet">8.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**CSS Architecture**</span> - Design systems and tokens
<span class="hljs-bullet">9.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**Browser APIs**</span> - localStorage, requestAnimationFrame
<span class="hljs-bullet">10.</span> <span class="hljs-strong">**UI/UX**</span> - Modern design patterns

<span class="hljs-section">## 2.4 Project Scope</span>

<span class="hljs-strong">**What&#x27;s Included:**</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Complete frontend application
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Mock data (no backend required)
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Responsive design
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Dark/light themes
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Shopping cart system
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Unit tests
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Professional documentation

<span class="hljs-strong">**What&#x27;s Not Included:**</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Backend API
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Payment processing
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> User authentication
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Database
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Email integration
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Video streaming

---

<span class="hljs-section"># 3. TECHNOLOGY STACK DEEP DIVE</span>

<span class="hljs-section">## 3.1 Frontend Framework</span>

<span class="hljs-section">### React 19.1.1</span>

<span class="hljs-strong">**What is React?**</span>

React is a declarative JavaScript library for building user interfaces using components. Instead of imperative DOM manipulation, you describe what the UI should look like, and React handles updates efficiently.

<span class="hljs-strong">**Why React 19?**</span>

<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Latest features and optimizations
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Improved hooks system
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Better TypeScript support
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Enhanced performance
<span class="hljs-bullet">-</span> Modern development experience

<span class="hljs-strong">**React Concepts Used:**</span>

<span class="hljs-code">```javascript
// 1. Functional Components
const Course = ({ course }) =&gt; {
  return &lt;article className=&quot;course-card&quot;&gt;...&lt;/article&gt;;
};

// 2. JSX - HTML-like syntax in JavaScript
return (
  &lt;div&gt;
    &lt;h1&gt;Course Title&lt;/h1&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;Price: ${price}&lt;/p&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
);

// 3. Props - Pass data to components
&lt;Course course={courseData} addToCart={handleAdd} /&gt;;

// 4. Hooks - Function-based state and effects
const [cart, setCart] = useState([]);
useEffect(() =&gt; {
  /* side effects */
}, [dependencies]);
```</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="react-dom-1911">React-DOM 19.1.1</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Connects React components to actual DOM</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { createRoot } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-dom/client&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> root = <span class="hljs-title function_">createRoot</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;root&quot;</span>));
root.<span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="32-router-react-router-dom-7132">3.2 Router: React Router DOM 7.13.2</h2>
<p><strong>Purpose:</strong> Client-side routing for SPA behavior</p>
<p><strong>Setup:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// main.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BrowserRouter</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;

<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">BrowserRouter</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">BrowserRouter</span>&gt;</span></span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// App.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">Routes</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">Route</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;

<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Routes</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Home</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/all&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">AllCourses</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/blog&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Blog</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">Routes</span>&gt;</span></span>;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Key Features:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>URL changes without page reload</li>
<li>Browser back/forward work correctly</li>
<li>Deep linking support</li>
<li>Dynamic route parameters</li>
<li>Nested routes</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="33-state-management-react-context-api">3.3 State Management: React Context API</h2>
<p><strong>Why Context API?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Built into React (no external dependency)</li>
<li>Perfect for medium complexity apps</li>
<li>Easier to learn than Redux</li>
<li>Sufficient for LearnHub's needs</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Architecture:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// 1. Create context</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_">createContext</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// 2. Create provider</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">CartProvider</span>(<span class="hljs-params">{ children }</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>([]);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> value = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(
    <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> ({
      cart,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartCount</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartTotal</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>),
      addToCart,
      removeFromCart,
      clearCart,
    }),
    [cart, addToCart, removeFromCart, clearCart],
  );

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span> <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{value}</span>&gt;</span>{children}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span>&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// 3. Create custom hook</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> ctx = <span class="hljs-title function_">useContext</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!ctx) <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;useCart must be within CartProvider&quot;</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ctx;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// 4. Use in components</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();
</code></pre>
<h2 id="34-build-tool-vite-rolldown-7114">3.4 Build Tool: Vite (Rolldown) 7.1.14</h2>
<p><strong>What is Vite?</strong></p>
<p>Modern build tool that provides:</p>
<ul>
<li>Instant server start (HMR)</li>
<li>Lightning-fast builds</li>
<li>Optimized production output</li>
<li>Native ES module support</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Development vs Production:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-bash"><span class="hljs-comment"># Development</span>
npm run dev
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Serves modules over HTTP</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Hot Module Replacement (HMR)</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Source maps for debugging</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - No minification</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Production</span>
npm run build
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Bundles all code</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Minifies JavaScript and CSS</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Optimizes images</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Generates source maps</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Creates /dist folder</span>
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Configuration:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vite.config.js</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { defineConfig } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vite&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> react <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@vitejs/plugin-react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">defineConfig</span>({
  <span class="hljs-attr">plugins</span>: [<span class="hljs-title function_">react</span>()], <span class="hljs-comment">// Enable JSX transformation</span>
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="35-styling-bootstrap-538--custom-css">3.5 Styling: Bootstrap 5.3.8 + Custom CSS</h2>
<h3 id="bootstrap-integration">Bootstrap Integration</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// main.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;bootstrap/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css&quot;</span>;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Bootstrap provides:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>12-column responsive grid</li>
<li>Utility classes (margins, padding, etc.)</li>
<li>Pre-built components</li>
<li>Responsive breakpoints</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="custom-css-with-variables">Custom CSS with Variables</h3>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* Design tokens in :root */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:root</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attr">--accent-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#3b82f6</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attr">--text-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#1e293b</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attr">--surface-page</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#f8fafc</span>;
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* ... many more variables */</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Dark mode override */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-tag">body</span><span class="hljs-selector-class">.dark-mode</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attr">--accent-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#60a5fa</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attr">--text-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#f8fafc</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attr">--surface-page</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#0f172a</span>;
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="36-notifications-react-toastify-1105">3.6 Notifications: React Toastify 11.0.5</h2>
<p><strong>Setup:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// main.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify/dist/ReactToastify.css&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">ToastContainer</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// App.jsx</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">ToastContainer</span> <span class="hljs-attr">position</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;bottom-center&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">autoClose</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{2800}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">theme</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;colored&quot;</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Usage:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { toast } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify&quot;</span>;

toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Added to cart!&quot;</span>);
toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Something went wrong&quot;</span>);
toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cart cleared&quot;</span>);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="37-testing-vitest-324--react-testing-library-1630">3.7 Testing: Vitest 3.2.4 + React Testing Library 16.3.0</h2>
<p><strong>Why Vitest?</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Jest-compatible API</li>
<li>Built on Vite (faster)</li>
<li>Modern testing experience</li>
<li>ESM support</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Configuration:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vitest.config.js</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">defineConfig</span>({
  <span class="hljs-attr">test</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">environment</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;jsdom&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// Simulate DOM</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">globals</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// Global test functions</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">setupFiles</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">&quot;./src/setupTests.js&quot;</span>],
  },
});
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Testing Pattern:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { render, screen } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@testing-library/react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { describe, test, expect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vitest&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-title function_">describe</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Course Component&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;renders course title&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{mockCourse}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByText</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;React Basics&quot;</span>)).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="38-code-quality-eslint-9360">3.8 Code Quality: ESLint 9.36.0</h2>

<h1 id="4-complete-project-architecture">4. COMPLETE PROJECT ARCHITECTURE</h1>
<h2 id="41-layered-architecture-pattern">4.1 Layered Architecture Pattern</h2>
<pre><code>┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                  PRESENTATION LAYER                      │
│              Pages (Home, Explore, Resources)            │
│          User-facing views rendered based on routes      │
└────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────┘
                     ↓
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                 COMPONENT LAYER                          │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐   │
│  │   Navbar     │  │    Cart      │  │   Course     │   │
│  │              │  │              │  │              │   │
│  │ Navigation   │  │ Shopping     │  │ Single       │   │
│  │ &amp; Theme      │  │ Cart UI      │  │ Course Card  │   │
│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘   │
└────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────┘
                     ↓
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│            STATE MANAGEMENT &amp; LOGIC LAYER                │
│                  CartContext.jsx                         │
│  • Global cart state                                     │
│  • Methods: addToCart, removeFromCart, clearCart         │
│  • localStorage persistence                             │
│  • Memoized calculations                                │
└────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────┘
                     ↓
┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                   DATA LAYER                             │
│  • fakeData.js (44 mock courses)                         │
│  • localStorage (cart persistence)                      │
│  • Browser APIs                                         │
└──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
</code></pre>
<h2 id="42-data-flow-diagram">4.2 Data Flow Diagram</h2>
<pre><code>USER ACTION
    ↓
Component Event Handler
    ↓
Call Context Function (addToCart, removeFromCart)
    ↓
State Update (setCart)
    ↓
useEffect Triggers
    ↓
Save to localStorage
    ↓
Component Re-render
    ↓
UI Updates
    ↓
User Sees Changes
</code></pre>
<h2 id="43-component-hierarchy">4.3 Component Hierarchy</h2>
<pre><code>App (Root)
  ├── CartProvider (Context Wrapper)
  │   └── AppShell
  │       ├── Navbar (sticky)
  │       │   ├── Logo
  │       │   ├── Desktop Navigation
  │       │   │   ├── Dropdown (Courses)
  │       │   │   └── Dropdown (Resources)
  │       │   ├── Theme Toggle
  │       │   ├── Cart Button
  │       │   ├── Mobile Drawer
  │       │   └── Cart Panel (slide-out)
  │       ├── Cart (horizontal layout)
  │       │   ├── Cart Items List
  │       │   └── Cart Summary
  │       └── Routes
  │           ├── Home
  │           │   └── CourseGrid
  │           │       └── Course Cards (44 total)
  │           ├── AllCourses
  │           ├── WebDevelopment
  │           ├── DataScience
  │           ├── CloudComputing
  │           ├── UiUxDesign
  │           ├── Blog
  │           ├── Community
  │           ├── SuccessStories
  │           ├── Documentation
  │           └── Instructors
  └── ToastContainer
</code></pre>

└── 📄 LEARNHUB_DOCUMENTATION.md     # Technical docs
</code></pre>
<h2 id="52-file-organization-rationale">5.2 File Organization Rationale</h2>
<p><strong>By Feature:</strong> Easier to find related code</p>
<ul>
<li>/Components/Navbar/ has Navbar.jsx AND Navbar.css together</li>
<li>Self-contained components with all dependencies</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>By Type:</strong> Separation of concerns</p>
<ul>
<li>/context for state management</li>
<li>/pages for route components</li>
<li>/styles for global styles</li>
<li>/fakeData for mock data</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Scalability:</strong> Easy to add features</p>
<ul>
<li>Add new page: Create folder in /pages</li>
<li>Add new component: Create folder in /Components</li>
<li>Add new state: Add to /context</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h1 id="6-html-entry-point">6. HTML ENTRY POINT</h1>
<h2 id="61-indexhtml">6.1 index.html</h2>

    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- 7. MAIN JAVASCRIPT ENTRY POINT --&gt;</span>

    <span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- Loads main.jsx which sets up entire React application --&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">script</span> <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;module&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">src</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/src/main.jsx&quot;</span>&gt;</span><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">script</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">body</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">html</span>&gt;</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="62-single-page-application-spa-concept">6.2 Single Page Application (SPA) Concept</h2>
<p><strong>Traditional Multi-Page App:</strong></p>
<pre><code>user visits /page1  → Browser loads page1.html
user clicks link    → Browser loads page2.html
user goes back      → Browser loads page1.html again
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Single Page App (SPA):</strong></p>
<pre><code>user visits /       → Browser loads index.html once
user clicks link    → JavaScript changes URL + renders new component
user goes back      → Browser button works, JavaScript renders original
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Benefits of SPA:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Faster navigation (no full page reload)</li>
<li>Smoother user experience</li>
<li>Can work offline with service workers</li>
<li>Only one HTML file to maintain</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="63-react-root-mounting">6.3 React Root Mounting</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// main.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { createRoot } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-dom/client&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">App</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./App.jsx&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Step 1: Get the root element</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> rootElement = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;root&quot;</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Step 2: Create React root</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> root = <span class="hljs-title function_">createRoot</span>(rootElement);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Step 3: Render React app into root</span>
root.<span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span></span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Result: React replaces everything in &lt;div id=&quot;root&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// with the App component</span>
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h1 id="7-css-architecture--design-system">7. CSS ARCHITECTURE &amp; DESIGN SYSTEM</h1>
<h2 id="71-design-tokens-css-variables">7.1 Design Tokens (CSS Variables)</h2>
<h3 id="purpose">Purpose</h3>
<p>Design tokens are reusable values that define the visual design system. Using CSS variables allows:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Single source of truth</strong> for colors, spacing, typography</li>
<li><strong>Easy theme switching</strong> (light/dark mode)</li>
<li><strong>Consistency</strong> across entire application</li>
<li><strong>Easy maintenance</strong> - change one variable, everything updates</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="color-system">Color System</h3>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:root</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* ──────────────────────────
     PRIMARY ACCENT COLORS
     ────────────────────────── */</span>

<h3 id="enabling-dark-mode">Enabling Dark Mode</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// In Navbar.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [darkMode, setDarkMode] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(
  <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;theme&quot;</span>) === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;dark&quot;</span>,
);

<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Add or remove dark-mode class from body</span>
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-property">body</span>.<span class="hljs-property">classList</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">toggle</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;dark-mode&quot;</span>, darkMode);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Persist preference</span>
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;theme&quot;</span>, darkMode ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;dark&quot;</span> : <span class="hljs-string">&quot;light&quot;</span>);
}, [darkMode]);

<span class="hljs-comment">// User sees theme change instantly across entire app</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="72-global-styles">7.2 Global Styles</h2>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* src/styles/index.css */</span>

<span class="hljs-selector-tag">body</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">margin</span>: <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Remove browser default margins */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">min-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">320px</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Minimum mobile width */</span>

  <span class="hljs-attribute">background-color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--surface-page);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">color</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--text-color);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">font-family</span>:
    <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Inter&quot;</span>,
    system-ui,
    -apple-system,
    <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Segoe UI&quot;</span>,
    Roboto,
    Arial,
    sans-serif;

  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Smooth transition when switching themes */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">transition</span>:
    background-color <span class="hljs-number">0.28s</span> ease,
    color <span class="hljs-number">0.28s</span> ease;
}
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-selector-class">.navbar-dropdown</span> {
  backdrop-<span class="hljs-attribute">filter</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">blur</span>(<span class="hljs-number">12px</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">/* Blur background */</span>
  -webkit-backdrop-<span class="hljs-attribute">filter</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">blur</span>(<span class="hljs-number">12px</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">/* Safari support */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">background</span>: <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--glass-bg); <span class="hljs-comment">/* Semi-transparent background */</span>

  <span class="hljs-attribute">border-radius</span>: <span class="hljs-number">12px</span>;
}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="gradient-text">Gradient Text</h3>

    <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-deep) <span class="hljs-number">0%</span>,
    <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-color) <span class="hljs-number">42%</span>,
    <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-violet) <span class="hljs-number">100%</span>
  );
  <span class="hljs-attribute">background-clip</span>: text; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Apply background to text */</span>
  -webkit-<span class="hljs-attribute">background-clip</span>: text;
  -webkit-text-fill-<span class="hljs-attribute">color</span>: transparent; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Show gradient through text */</span>

  }

  }
