<h1 id="8-javascript--react-fundamentals">8. JAVASCRIPT &amp; REACT FUNDAMENTALS</h1>
<h2 id="81-es6-features">8.1 ES6+ Features</h2>
<h3 id="arrow-functions">Arrow Functions</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Traditional function</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span>(<span class="hljs-params">a, b</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> a + b;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Arrow function (cleaner)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">a, b</span>) =&gt; a + b;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Arrow function with block body</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">add</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">a, b</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> result = a + b;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> result;
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// In React components</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleClick</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Clicked!&quot;</span>);
};
</code></pre>
<h3 id="destructuring">Destructuring</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Object destructuring</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { title, price, instructor } = course;
<span class="hljs-comment">// Instead of: const title = course.title; const price = course.price;</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Array destructuring</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [first, second] = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>];

<span class="hljs-comment">// In function parameters</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Course</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">{ course, addToCart }</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// course and addToCart are automatically extracted</span>
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// Default values</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { isDark = <span class="hljs-literal">false</span> } = settings;
</code></pre>
<h3 id="spread-operator-">Spread Operator (...)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Array spreading</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> original = [<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>];
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> copy = [...original]; <span class="hljs-comment">// [1, 2, 3]</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Combining arrays</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> combined = [...arr1, ...arr2];

<span class="hljs-comment">// Adding to array (immutable)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> newItems = [...cart, newCourse];

<span class="hljs-comment">// Object spreading</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> updated = { ...user, <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;John&quot;</span> };

<span class="hljs-comment">// In cart context - spread to avoid mutation</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([...cart, newCourse]);
</code></pre>
<h3 id="template-literals">Template Literals</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// String concatenation</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> old = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Hello &quot;</span> + name + <span class="hljs-string">&quot;!&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Template literal (cleaner)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> modern = <span class="hljs-string">`Hello <span class="hljs-subst">${name}</span>!`</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Multi-line strings</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> message = <span class="hljs-string">`
  Welcome to <span class="hljs-subst">${siteName}</span>
  Your order total: $<span class="hljs-subst">${total}</span>
`</span>;
</code></pre>
<h3 id="ternary-operator">Ternary Operator</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Simple if-else</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> status = isEnrolled ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Enrolled&quot;</span> : <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Not enrolled&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Nested ternary (harder to read)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> color =
  status === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;active&quot;</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;green&quot;</span> : status === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;pending&quot;</span> ? <span class="hljs-string">&quot;yellow&quot;</span> : <span class="hljs-string">&quot;red&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Better: Use if-else for complex logic</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="optional-chaining-">Optional Chaining (?.)</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Safely access nested properties</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> name = user?.<span class="hljs-property">profile</span>?.<span class="hljs-property">name</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// If user is null/undefined, returns undefined (no error)</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Instead of: user &amp;&amp; user.profile &amp;&amp; user.profile.name</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="array-methods">Array Methods</h3>
<h4 id="map---transform">map() - Transform</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Transform each course into a Component</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> courseElements = courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> (
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course.id}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>
));

<span class="hljs-comment">// Each item transformed</span>
[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>].<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">n</span>) =&gt;</span> n * <span class="hljs-number">2</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// [2, 4, 6]</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="filter---remove-items-1">filter() - Remove Items</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Remove course from cart</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">removeFromCart</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">id</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">filter</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> !== id));
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns new array without matching items</span>
[<span class="hljs-number">1</span>, <span class="hljs-number">2</span>, <span class="hljs-number">3</span>, <span class="hljs-number">4</span>].<span class="hljs-title function_">filter</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">n</span>) =&gt;</span> n &gt; <span class="hljs-number">2</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// [3, 4]</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="reduce---aggregate">reduce() - Aggregate</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Calculate total price</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> total = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Starts with sum = 0</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// For each item: sum = sum + item.price</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// [10, 20, 30].reduce((sum, n) =&gt; sum + n, 0) = 60</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="some---check-any">some() - Check Any</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Check if already in cart</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> isEnrolled = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">some</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === courseId);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns true if ANY item matches</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns false if NO items match</span>
</code></pre>
<h4 id="find---get-first-match">find() - Get First Match</h4>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Find specific course</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> course = courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">find</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">c</span>) =&gt;</span> c.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Returns first matching item or undefined</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="82-react-hooks">8.2 React Hooks</h2>
<h3 id="usestate---state-management-1">useState - State Management</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useState } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Component</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Declare state: [currentValue, updateFunction]</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>([]);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [count, setCount] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [darkMode, setDarkMode] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">false</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// cart = [] initially</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// setCart = function to update cart</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Update state</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">addItem</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([...cart, item]); <span class="hljs-comment">// Component re-renders</span>
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Conditional rendering based on state</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>{cart.length === 0 ? <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>Empty<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span> : <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>Items: {cart.length}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="useeffect---side-effects-1">useEffect - Side Effects</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useEffect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Component</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Component mounted or deps changed&quot;</span>);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Side effects:</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">// - Fetch data from API</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">// - Save to localStorage</span>
    <span class="hljs-comment">// - Subscribe to events</span>

    <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;data&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(data));

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Optional cleanup function</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
      <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cleanup before re-effect&quot;</span>);
      <span class="hljs-comment">// Unsubscribe, cancel requests, etc.</span>
    };
  }, [dependencies]); <span class="hljs-comment">// Re-run when dependencies change</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Dependency array options:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// []           - Run once on mount</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// [variable]   - Run when variable changes</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// (omitted)    - Run after every render (avoid!)</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="usecontext---global-state">useContext - Global State</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useContext } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./context&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Component</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Get global context value</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart, removeFromCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useContext</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Can now use global state</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>{cart.length} items<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Better: Use custom hook</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();
</code></pre>
<h3 id="usecallback---memoize-functions-1">useCallback - Memoize Functions</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useCallback } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Component</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Without useCallback - NEW function every render</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleClick_bad</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">doSomething</span>();
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// With useCallback - SAME function unless deps change</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> handleClick = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">doSomething</span>();
  }, [dependencies]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Benefits:</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Function reference stays same</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Child components don&#x27;t unnecessarily re-render</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Better performance with memoized children</span>
}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="usememo---memoize-values">useMemo - Memoize Values</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useMemo } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Component</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Without useMemo - Calculated every render</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> total_bad = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// With useMemo - Calculated only when deps change</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> total = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
  }, [cart]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Benefits:</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Expensive calculations run fewer times</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Value reference stays same</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// - Better performance</span>
}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="useref---reference-to-dom">useRef - Reference to DOM</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useRef } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Component</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> inputRef = <span class="hljs-title function_">useRef</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleFocus</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Access DOM element directly</span>
    inputRef.<span class="hljs-property">current</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">focus</span>();
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">input</span> <span class="hljs-attr">ref</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{inputRef}</span> /&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span> <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{handleFocus}</span>&gt;</span>Focus<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/&gt;</span></span>
  );
}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="custom-hook-usecart">Custom Hook: useCart</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// src/context/CartContext.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> {
  createContext,
  useContext,
  useState,
  useCallback,
  useMemo,
  useEffect,
} <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_">createContext</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">CartProvider</span>(<span class="hljs-params">{ children }</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Initialize from localStorage</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> saved = <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> saved ? <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(saved) : [];
  });

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Save to localStorage whenever cart changes</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(cart));
  }, [cart]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Add course to cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> addToCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> {
      <span class="hljs-comment">// Check if already exists</span>
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (prev.<span class="hljs-title function_">some</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>)) {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> prev; <span class="hljs-comment">// Don&#x27;t add duplicate</span>
      }
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [...prev, course];
    });
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Remove course from cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> removeFromCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">id</span>) =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> prev.<span class="hljs-title function_">filter</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> !== id));
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Clear entire cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> clearCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([]);
  }, []);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Memoized context value</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> value = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(
    <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> ({
      cart,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartCount</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>,
      <span class="hljs-attr">cartTotal</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + <span class="hljs-title class_">Number</span>(item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>), <span class="hljs-number">0</span>),
      addToCart,
      removeFromCart,
      clearCart,
    }),
    [cart, addToCart, removeFromCart, clearCart],
  );

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span> <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{value}</span>&gt;</span>{children}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">CartContext.Provider</span>&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Custom hook to use cart context</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> ctx = <span class="hljs-title function_">useContext</span>(<span class="hljs-title class_">CartContext</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!ctx) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;useCart must be used within CartProvider&quot;</span>);
  }
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> ctx;
}
</code></pre>

<h1 id="9-components-breakdown">9. COMPONENTS BREAKDOWN</h1>
<h2 id="91-coursejsx---course-card-component">9.1 Course.jsx - Course Card Component</h2>
<p><strong>Size:</strong> 1.5 KB | <strong>Lines:</strong> 49 | <strong>Complexity:</strong> Simple</p>
<p><strong>Purpose:</strong> Display individual course with add-to-cart button</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { toast } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useCart } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;../../context/CartContext&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./Course.css&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Course</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">{ course }</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Destructure course properties</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { title, instructor, price, img } = course;

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Get cart functions from context</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, addToCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Check if course already in cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-comment">// array.some() returns true if ANY item matches the condition</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> isEnrolled = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">some</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Format price to 2 decimal places</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> priceLabel =
    <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> price === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;number&quot;</span> ? price.<span class="hljs-title function_">toFixed</span>(<span class="hljs-number">2</span>) : <span class="hljs-title class_">String</span>(price);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Handle enrollment button click</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleEnroll</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (isEnrolled) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// Prevent duplicate adds</span>
    <span class="hljs-title function_">addToCart</span>(course);
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">`Added to cart: <span class="hljs-subst">${title}</span>`</span>); <span class="hljs-comment">// Notify user</span>
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Render course card</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">article</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
      {/* Image section */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__media&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">img</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__img&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">src</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{img}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">alt</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;&quot;</span> /&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

      {/* Content section */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__body&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        {/* Title */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">h3</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__title&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{title}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">h3</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Instructor info */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__instructor&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          Instructor
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__instructor-name&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{instructor}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Price and button */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__footer&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__price&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
            Price
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__price-value&quot;</span>&gt;</span>${priceLabel}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>

          {/* Button - disabled if already in cart */}
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-card__cta&quot;</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{handleEnroll}</span>
            <span class="hljs-attr">disabled</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{isEnrolled}</span>
          &gt;</span>
            {isEnrolled ? &quot;In cart&quot; : &quot;Add to cart&quot;}
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span></span>
  );
};

<h2 id="92-cartjsx---shopping-cart-display">9.2 Cart.jsx - Shopping Cart Display</h2>
<p><strong>Size:</strong> 4.1 KB | <strong>Lines:</strong> 132 | <strong>Complexity:</strong> Medium</p>
<p><strong>Purpose:</strong> Display cart contents and handle cart operations</p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useEffect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">Link</span>, useLocation, useNavigate } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { toast } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-toastify&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { useCart } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;../../context/CartContext&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./Cart.css&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-variable constant_">CART_ANCHOR</span> = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;learning-cart&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">Cart</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Get cart context</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> { cart, cartTotal, removeFromCart, clearCart } = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCart</span>();

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Router hooks</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> location = <span class="hljs-title function_">useLocation</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// Current route</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> navigate = <span class="hljs-title function_">useNavigate</span>(); <span class="hljs-comment">// Change route</span>

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Effect - Scroll to cart if URL has #learning-cart</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (location.<span class="hljs-property">hash</span> !== <span class="hljs-string">`#<span class="hljs-subst">${CART_ANCHOR}</span>`</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> el = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-variable constant_">CART_ANCHOR</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!el) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Use requestAnimationFrame for smooth scrolling</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> id = <span class="hljs-title function_">requestAnimationFrame</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
      el.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">behavior</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">block</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;start&quot;</span> });
    });

    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">cancelAnimationFrame</span>(id);
  }, [location.<span class="hljs-property">pathname</span>, location.<span class="hljs-property">hash</span>]);

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Handle clear cart with confirmation</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleClear</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;

    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (
      <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span> !== <span class="hljs-string">&quot;undefined&quot;</span> &amp;&amp;
      !<span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">confirm</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Remove all courses from your cart?&quot;</span>)
    ) {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span>;
    }

    <span class="hljs-title function_">clearCart</span>();
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">info</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cart cleared&quot;</span>);
  };

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Handle remove single item</span>
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleRemoveOne</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">removeFromCart</span>(course.<span class="hljs-property">id</span>);
    toast.<span class="hljs-title function_">success</span>(<span class="hljs-string">`Removed &quot;<span class="hljs-subst">${course.title}</span>&quot; from cart`</span>);
  };

  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">section</span>
      <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{CART_ANCHOR}</span>
      <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;horizontal-cart&quot;</span>
      <span class="hljs-attr">aria-labelledby</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-heading&quot;</span>
    &gt;</span>
      {/* Left section - Items list */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-left&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        {/* Header with title and count */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-heading-row&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">h2</span> <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-heading&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-title&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-hidden</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;true&quot;</span>&gt;</span>🛒<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span> My cart
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">h2</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-count-pill&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-live</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;polite&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
            {cart.length === 0
              ? &quot;0 courses&quot;
              : `${cart.length} course${cart.length === 1 ? &quot;&quot; : &quot;s&quot;}`}
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Items or empty state */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-items-container&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          {cart.length === 0 ? (
            // Empty cart
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-empty-block&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">p</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-empty&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Your cart is empty.<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">p</span>&gt;</span>
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Link</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-empty-cta&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">to</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                Browse courses
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">Link</span>&gt;</span>
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
          ) : (
            // List of cart items
            cart.map((course) =&gt; (
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course.id}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip course-chip--rich&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip__text&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip__title&quot;</span>&gt;</span>{course.title}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;course-chip__meta&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
                    {course.instructor} · ${Number(course.price).toFixed(2)}
                  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
                  <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;remove-btn&quot;</span>
                  <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{()</span> =&gt;</span> handleRemoveOne(course)}
                  title=&quot;Remove from cart&quot;
                  aria-label={`Remove ${course.title} from cart`}
                &gt;
                  ✕
                <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
            ))
          )}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

      {/* Right section - Summary and actions */}
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-right&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
        {/* Total price */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-right-summary&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-total-label&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Estimated total<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
          <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-total-price&quot;</span>&gt;</span>${cartTotal.toFixed(2)}<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span>
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>

        {/* Action buttons */}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-actions&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
          {cart.length &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; (
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;&gt;</span>
              {/* Clear cart button */}
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-btn-secondary&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{handleClear}</span>
              &gt;</span>
                Clear cart
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>

              {/* Checkout button (disabled in demo) */}
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-btn-checkout&quot;</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">disabled</span>
                <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Checkout not available in demo&quot;</span>
              &gt;</span>
                Checkout
              <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/&gt;</span>
          )}

          {/* Back to catalog (shown if not on home) */}
          {location.pathname !== &quot;/&quot; &amp;&amp; (
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span>
              <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>
              <span class="hljs-attr">className</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;cart-btn-text&quot;</span>
              <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{()</span> =&gt;</span> navigate({ pathname: &quot;/&quot;, hash: CART_ANCHOR })}
            &gt;
              Back to catalog
            <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
          )}
        <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
    &lt;/section&gt;
  );
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>Features:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Display all cart items</li>
<li>Show cart total</li>
<li>Remove individual items</li>
<li>Clear entire cart</li>
<li>Empty state handling</li>
<li>Smooth scrolling</li>
<li>Responsive layout</li>
</ul>

);

<li>Slide-out drawer</li>
<li>Same navigation items as desktop</li>

</ul>

<p><strong>Cart Panel</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Slide-out from right</li>

</ul>
</li>

<h1 id="10-state-management-in-detail">10. STATE MANAGEMENT IN DETAIL</h1>
<h2 id="101-context-api-architecture">10.1 Context API Architecture</h2>
<pre><code>┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│          CartContext.jsx                │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 1. Create Context                       │
│    const CartContext = createContext()  │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 2. Create Provider                      │
│    export function CartProvider()       │
│    • Initialize state from localStorage │
│    • Define methods (add, remove, etc)  │
│    • Provide context to children        │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 3. Create Custom Hook                   │
│    export function useCart()            │
│    • Get context value                  │
│    • Error handling                     │
│    • Easy to use in components          │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
</code></pre>
<h2 id="102-complete-flow">10.2 Complete Flow</h2>
<pre><code>User adds course
        ↓
Course.jsx → handleEnroll()
        ↓
Calls useCart().addToCart(course)
        ↓
CartContext.addToCart()
        ↓
Checks: Is course already in cart?
        ↓
If YES: return unchanged cart
If NO: setCart([...cart, course])
        ↓
Component re-renders
        ↓
useEffect saves to localStorage
        ↓
All components using useCart() re-render
        ↓
• Course button changes to &quot;In cart&quot;
• Cart count badge updates
• Navbar cart panel shows new item
• Cart section shows new total
        ↓
Toast notification: &quot;Added to cart&quot;
</code></pre>
<h2 id="103-localstorage-persistence">10.3 localStorage Persistence</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Save function</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(cart));
  } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (error) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Handle quota exceeded or private mode</span>
    <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Failed to save cart&quot;</span>);
  }
}, [cart]);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Load function</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">loadCartFromStorage</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> raw = <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!raw) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [];

    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> parsed = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(raw);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Array</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">isArray</span>(parsed) ? parsed : [];
  } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (error) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// If corrupted, return empty</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [];
  }
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Initialize state with loaded data</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(loadCartFromStorage);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="104-performance-optimization">10.4 Performance Optimization</h2>
<h3 id="usecallback---prevent-function-recreation-1">useCallback - Prevent Function Recreation</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Without memoization (bad for performance)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">addToCart_bad</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>([...cart, course]);
};
<span class="hljs-comment">// New function created every render</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Child components think function changed and re-render</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// With memoization (good)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> addToCart = <span class="hljs-title function_">useCallback</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">setCart</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">prev</span>) =&gt;</span> [...prev, course]);
}, []); <span class="hljs-comment">// Empty deps - function never changes</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Child components receive same function reference</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="usememo---prevent-expensive-calculations-1">useMemo - Prevent Expensive Calculations</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Without memoization (bad)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartPricing_bad = {
  <span class="hljs-attr">subtotal</span>: cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(...),
  <span class="hljs-attr">discount</span>: <span class="hljs-title function_">calculateDiscount</span>(...),
  <span class="hljs-attr">total</span>: <span class="hljs-title function_">calculateTotal</span>(...)
};
<span class="hljs-comment">// Recalculated every render</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// With memoization (good)</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> cartPricing = <span class="hljs-title function_">useMemo</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> subtotal = cart.<span class="hljs-title function_">reduce</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">sum, item</span>) =&gt;</span> sum + item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> discount = subtotal &gt;= <span class="hljs-number">100</span> ? subtotal * <span class="hljs-number">0.08</span> : <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> total = subtotal - discount + <span class="hljs-number">2.99</span>;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> { subtotal, discount, total };
}, [cart]);
<span class="hljs-comment">// Only recalculated when cart changes</span>
</code></pre>

<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Routes</span>&gt;</span>
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Home</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/all&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">AllCourses</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/web-development&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">WebDevelopment</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/data-science&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">DataScience</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/cloud-computing&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">CloudComputing</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/ui-ux-design&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">UiUxDesign</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;
  <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Route</span> <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/resources/blog&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">element</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{</span>&lt;<span class="hljs-attr">Blog</span> /&gt;</span>} /&gt;

  Home

<h2 id="114-hash-navigation-scroll-anchor">11.4 Hash Navigation (Scroll Anchor)</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Navigate to cart and scroll smoothly</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">goToCart</span> = (<span class="hljs-params"></span>) =&gt; {
  <span class="hljs-title function_">navigate</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">pathname</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">hash</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;learning-cart&quot;</span> });
};

<span class="hljs-comment">// Effect watches for hash change</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (location.<span class="hljs-property">hash</span> === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;#learning-cart&quot;</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> element = <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getElementById</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learning-cart&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (element) {
      element.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">behavior</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span> });
    }
  }
}, [location.<span class="hljs-property">hash</span>]);
</code></pre>
<hr>

<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// vitest.config.js</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { defineConfig } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vitest/config&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> react <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@vitejs/plugin-react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">export</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">default</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">defineConfig</span>({
  <span class="hljs-attr">plugins</span>: [<span class="hljs-title function_">react</span>()],
  <span class="hljs-attr">test</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">environment</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;jsdom&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// Simulate browser DOM</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">globals</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>, <span class="hljs-comment">// describe, test, etc. are global</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">setupFiles</span>: [<span class="hljs-string">&quot;./src/setupTests.js&quot;</span>],
  },
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="122-testing-example">12.2 Testing Example</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// src/App.test.jsx</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { render, screen } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;@testing-library/react&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { describe, test, expect } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;vitest&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">MemoryRouter</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react-router-dom&quot;</span>;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">App</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./App.jsx&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>(<span class="hljs-params">initialPath = <span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">render</span>(
    <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">MemoryRouter</span> <span class="hljs-attr">initialEntries</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{[initialPath]}</span>&gt;</span>
      <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">App</span> /&gt;</span>
    <span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">MemoryRouter</span>&gt;</span></span>,
  );
}

<span class="hljs-title function_">describe</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Online Learning App&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// Test 1: Cart heading renders</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;renders My Cart heading&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>();
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(
      screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByRole</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;heading&quot;</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-regexp">/my cart/i</span> }),
    ).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Test 2: Courses display</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;renders at least one course on home&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getByText</span>(<span class="hljs-regexp">/Complete Linux Training/i</span>)).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeInTheDocument</span>();
  });

  <span class="hljs-comment">// Test 3: Add to cart button</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">test</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Add to cart button is present&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
    <span class="hljs-title function_">renderApp</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> buttons = screen.<span class="hljs-title function_">getAllByRole</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>, { <span class="hljs-attr">name</span>: <span class="hljs-regexp">/add to cart/i</span> });
    <span class="hljs-title function_">expect</span>(buttons.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>).<span class="hljs-title function_">toBeGreaterThan</span>(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
  });
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="123-running-tests">12.3 Running Tests</h2>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Run tests in watch mode</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Run specific test file</span>
npm run <span class="hljs-built_in">test</span> -- Course.test.jsx

<h1 id="13-performance-optimization">13. PERFORMANCE OPTIMIZATION</h1>
<h2 id="131-react-performance">13.1 React Performance</h2>
<h3 id="code-splitting">Code Splitting</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Routes automatically code-split</span>
&lt;<span class="hljs-title class_">Route</span> path=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;/explore/web-development&quot;</span> element={<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">WebDevelopment</span> /&gt;</span></span>} /&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// WebDevelopment component loads only when user navigates to /explore/web-development</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Reduces initial bundle size</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="memoization">Memoization</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Prevent unnecessary re-renders of child components</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { memo } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;react&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Course</span> = <span class="hljs-title function_">memo</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">{ course, addToCart }</span>) =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span>...<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span></span>;
});

<span class="hljs-comment">// Course only re-renders if course or addToCart props change</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="key-optimization">Key Optimization</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Always use unique, stable keys in lists</span>
{
  courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course.id}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// WRONG - using index</span>
{
  courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course, index</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{index}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Using index as key causes issues:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - If list is reordered, component state gets mixed up</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - If items are added/removed, state becomes incorrect</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Performance suffers</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="132-vite-build-optimization">13.2 Vite Build Optimization</h2>
<pre><code class="language-bash"><span class="hljs-comment"># Build produces optimized output</span>
npm run build

<span class="hljs-comment"># Creates /dist with:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Minified JavaScript</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Minified CSS</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Optimized images</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Source maps for debugging</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># - Tree-shaken unused code</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="133-image-optimization">13.3 Image Optimization</h2>
<pre><code class="language-jsx"><span class="hljs-comment">// Using CDN for icons</span>
&lt;img
  src=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/devicons/devicon/icons/react/react-original.svg&quot;</span>
  alt=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;React icon&quot;</span>
  decoding=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;async&quot;</span>  <span class="hljs-comment">// Async image loading</span>
/&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// CSS image optimization</span>
.<span class="hljs-property">course</span>-card__img {
  <span class="hljs-attr">width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">100</span>%;
  <span class="hljs-attr">height</span>: 120px;
  object-<span class="hljs-attr">fit</span>: contain;  <span class="hljs-comment">// Scale without distortion</span>
  object-<span class="hljs-attr">position</span>: center;
}
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h1 id="14-accessibility--ux">14. ACCESSIBILITY &amp; UX</h1>
<h2 id="141-semantic-html-1">14.1 Semantic HTML</h2>
<pre><code class="language-html"><span class="hljs-comment">&lt;!-- Use meaningful tags --&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">nav</span>&gt;</span>Navigation area<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">nav</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span>Course card<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">article</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">section</span>&gt;</span>Cart section<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">section</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span> <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;button&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Action button<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">label</span> <span class="hljs-attr">for</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;input&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Input label<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">label</span>&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">input</span> <span class="hljs-attr">id</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;input&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-label</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Additional label&quot;</span> /&gt;</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="142-aria-labels-1">14.2 ARIA Labels</h2>
<pre><code class="language-jsx"><span class="hljs-comment">// Screen reader labels</span>
&lt;button aria-label=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Add to cart&quot;</span>&gt;+&lt;/button&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Live regions for dynamic updates</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">span</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-live</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;polite&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-atomic</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;true&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
  {cartCount} items in cart
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">span</span>&gt;</span></span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Descriptions</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-labelledby</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;heading-id&quot;</span>&gt;</span>Content<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Dialog/modal</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">role</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;dialog&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-modal</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;true&quot;</span> <span class="hljs-attr">aria-label</span>=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Shopping cart&quot;</span>&gt;</span>
  ...
<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">div</span>&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="143-keyboard-navigation-1">14.3 Keyboard Navigation</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Handle Escape key</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleKeyDown</span> = (<span class="hljs-params">e</span>) =&gt; {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (e.<span class="hljs-property">key</span> === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Escape&quot;</span>) {
      <span class="hljs-title function_">closeMenus</span>();
    }
  };
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">addEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;keydown&quot;</span>, handleKeyDown);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">document</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">removeEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;keydown&quot;</span>, handleKeyDown);
}, []);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Tab navigation works automatically with proper HTML</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Links and buttons are focusable</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Form inputs are focusable</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Tab order follows DOM order</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="144-focus-indicators">14.4 Focus Indicators</h2>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* Visible focus indicators for keyboard users */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-tag">button</span><span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:focus</span>-visible {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">outline</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2px</span> solid <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-color);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">outline-offset</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2px</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attribute">border-radius</span>: <span class="hljs-number">4px</span>;
}

<span class="hljs-selector-tag">a</span><span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:focus</span>-visible {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">outline</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2px</span> solid <span class="hljs-built_in">var</span>(--accent-color);
  <span class="hljs-attribute">outline-offset</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2px</span>;
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="145-color-contrast">14.5 Color Contrast</h2>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* WCAG AA Compliant (4.5:1 ratio minimum) */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-pseudo">:root</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Dark text on light background: 16.47:1 */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attr">--text-color</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#1e293b</span>;
  <span class="hljs-attr">--surface-page</span>: <span class="hljs-number">#f8fafc</span>;

  <span class="hljs-comment">/* Light text on dark background */</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Tested with tools like WebAIM Contrast Checker */</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="146-responsive-design-for-all-users">14.6 Responsive Design for All Users</h2>
<pre><code class="language-css"><span class="hljs-comment">/* Larger touch targets for mobile */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-tag">button</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">min-height</span>: <span class="hljs-number">44px</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Recommended for touch */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">min-width</span>: <span class="hljs-number">44px</span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Font size readable for users with low vision */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-tag">body</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">font-size</span>: <span class="hljs-number">16px</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Not too small */</span>
  <span class="hljs-attribute">line-height</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1.5</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Readable line spacing */</span>
}

<span class="hljs-comment">/* Sufficient spacing between interactive elements */</span>
<span class="hljs-selector-class">.navbar-links</span> {
  <span class="hljs-attribute">gap</span>: <span class="hljs-number">2rem</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">/* Space between links */</span>
}
</code></pre>
