<h1 id="16-security-considerations">16. SECURITY CONSIDERATIONS</h1>
<h2 id="161-xss-prevention">16.1 XSS Prevention</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// React sanitizes JSX by default</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Safe - HTML-escaped automatically</span>
&lt;div&gt;{userInput}&lt;/div&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// NEVER use dangerouslySetInnerHTML</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// UNSAFE - Can execute malicious code</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">div</span> <span class="hljs-attr">dangerouslySetInnerHTML</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{{__html:</span> <span class="hljs-attr">userInput</span>}} /&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="162-localstorage-safety">16.2 localStorage Safety</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Validate data from localStorage</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">loadCartFromStorage</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> raw = <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;learnhub-cart&quot;</span>);
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!raw) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [];

    <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> parsed = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(raw);

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Validate it&#x27;s an array</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!<span class="hljs-title class_">Array</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">isArray</span>(parsed)) <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [];

    <span class="hljs-comment">// Validate each item</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> parsed.<span class="hljs-title function_">filter</span>(
      <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">item</span>) =&gt;</span>
        item &amp;&amp; <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">id</span> === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;number&quot;</span> &amp;&amp; <span class="hljs-keyword">typeof</span> item.<span class="hljs-property">price</span> === <span class="hljs-string">&quot;number&quot;</span>,
    );
  } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (error) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// If corrupted, return empty</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> [];
  }
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="163-no-sensitive-data-storage">16.3 No Sensitive Data Storage</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// NEVER store in localStorage or cookies:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// ❌ Passwords</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// ❌ Auth tokens (use httpOnly cookies instead)</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// ❌ API keys</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// ❌ Personal information</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// LearnHub stores only:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// ✅ Cart data (mock/demo)</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// ✅ Theme preference</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// ✅ Public course information</span>
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h1 id="17-browser-apis-used">17. BROWSER APIs USED</h1>
<h2 id="171-localstorage">17.1 localStorage</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Save data</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;key&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">stringify</span>(data));

<span class="hljs-comment">// Load data</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> data = <span class="hljs-title class_">JSON</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">parse</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;key&quot;</span>));

<span class="hljs-comment">// Remove specific item</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">removeItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;key&quot;</span>);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Clear all</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">clear</span>();

<span class="hljs-comment">// Check storage</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-property">length</span>);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="172-requestanimationframe">17.2 requestAnimationFrame</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Smooth scrolling</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> id = <span class="hljs-title function_">requestAnimationFrame</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  element.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">behavior</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span> });
});

<span class="hljs-comment">// Cancel animation frame</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">cancelAnimationFrame</span>(id);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="173-windowconfirm">17.3 window.confirm()</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Ask user for confirmation</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (<span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">confirm</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Are you sure?&quot;</span>)) {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// User clicked OK</span>
  <span class="hljs-title function_">deleteItem</span>();
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
  <span class="hljs-comment">// User clicked Cancel</span>
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="174-windowmatchmedia">17.4 window.matchMedia()</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Check if user prefers dark mode</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> darkModePreferred = <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">matchMedia</span>(
  <span class="hljs-string">&quot;(prefers-color-scheme: dark)&quot;</span>,
).<span class="hljs-property">matches</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Listen for changes</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> mediaQuery = <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">matchMedia</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;(prefers-color-scheme: dark)&quot;</span>);
mediaQuery.<span class="hljs-title function_">addEventListener</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;change&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">e</span>) =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (e.<span class="hljs-property">matches</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// Dark mode enabled</span>
  }
});
</code></pre>
<h2 id="175-elementscrollintoview">17.5 Element.scrollIntoView()</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Scroll element into view</span>
element.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>();

<span class="hljs-comment">// Smooth scroll</span>
element.<span class="hljs-title function_">scrollIntoView</span>({ <span class="hljs-attr">behavior</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-attr">block</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;start&quot;</span> });

<span class="hljs-comment">// Options:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - behavior: &quot;auto&quot; | &quot;smooth&quot;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - block: &quot;start&quot; | &quot;center&quot; | &quot;end&quot; | &quot;nearest&quot;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - inline: &quot;start&quot; | &quot;center&quot; | &quot;end&quot; | &quot;nearest&quot;</span>
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h1 id="18-common-react-patterns">18. COMMON REACT PATTERNS</h1>
<h2 id="181-controlled-components-1">18.1 Controlled Components</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Input controlled by React state</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [value, setValue] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;&quot;</span>);

<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> (
  <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">input</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">value</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{value}</span>
    <span class="hljs-attr">onChange</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{(e)</span> =&gt;</span> setValue(e.target.value)}
    placeholder=&quot;Type here...&quot;
  /&gt;</span>
);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Benefits:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - React is source of truth</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Can validate input</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Easy to reset</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Can disable/enable dynamically</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="182-conditional-rendering-1">18.2 Conditional Rendering</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Method 1: If-else</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">EmptyCart</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
} <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartItems</span> <span class="hljs-attr">items</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{cart}</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Method 2: Ternary operator</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> === <span class="hljs-number">0</span> ? <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">EmptyCart</span> /&gt;</span></span> : <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartItems</span> /&gt;</span></span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Method 3: Logical AND</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> cart.<span class="hljs-property">length</span> &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span> &amp;&amp; <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">CartItems</span> /&gt;</span></span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Method 4: Switch statement</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">switch</span> (status) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;loading&quot;</span>:
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Loading</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;error&quot;</span>:
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Error</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">case</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;success&quot;</span>:
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Success</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
  <span class="hljs-attr">default</span>:
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Nothing</span> /&gt;</span></span>;
}
</code></pre>
<h2 id="183-rendering-lists">18.3 Rendering Lists</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Correct - unique key for each item</span>
{
  courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course.id}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// WRONG - using index as key</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Causes bugs when list changes</span>
{
  courses.<span class="hljs-title function_">map</span>(<span class="hljs-function">(<span class="hljs-params">course, index</span>) =&gt;</span> <span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">Course</span> <span class="hljs-attr">key</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{index}</span> <span class="hljs-attr">course</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{course}</span> /&gt;</span></span>);
}

<span class="hljs-comment">// Key requirements:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Must be unique among siblings</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Must be stable (same for same item)</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Cannot be position/index</span>
</code></pre>
<h2 id="184-event-handling-1">18.4 Event Handling</h2>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Method 1: Arrow function in JSX</span>
&lt;button onClick={<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">handleClick</span>(id)}&gt;<span class="hljs-title class_">Click</span>&lt;/button&gt;

<span class="hljs-comment">// Method 2: Call handler directly</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">button</span> <span class="hljs-attr">onClick</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{handleClick}</span>&gt;</span>Click<span class="hljs-tag">&lt;/<span class="hljs-name">button</span>&gt;</span></span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Method 3: Get event object</span>
<span class="language-xml"><span class="hljs-tag">&lt;<span class="hljs-name">input</span> <span class="hljs-attr">onChange</span>=<span class="hljs-string">{(e)</span> =&gt;</span> setValue(e.target.value)} /&gt;</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Event Pooling (React 16.x) - NOT in React 17+</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// If you need event in async code, call e.persist()</span>
</code></pre>

<h1 id="20-troubleshooting-guide">20. TROUBLESHOOTING GUIDE</h1>
<h2 id="201-common-issues">20.1 Common Issues</h2>
<h3 id="issue-changes-not-reflecting-in-browser">Issue: Changes not reflecting in browser</h3>
<p><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-bash"><span class="hljs-comment"># Clear npm cache</span>
npm cache clean --force

<span class="hljs-comment"># Reinstall dependencies</span>
<span class="hljs-built_in">rm</span> -rf node_modules
npm install

<span class="hljs-comment"># Restart dev server</span>
npm run dev
</code></pre>
<h3 id="issue-localstorage-not-persisting">Issue: localStorage not persisting</h3>
<p><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Check browser storage is enabled</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Ensure not in private/incognito mode</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Check storage quota isn&#x27;t exceeded</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Verify JSON serialization works</span>

<span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;test&quot;</span>, <span class="hljs-string">&quot;test&quot;</span>);
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">localStorage</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">removeItem</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;test&quot;</span>);
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Storage works&quot;</span>);
} <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (e) {
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">error</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Storage error:&quot;</span>, e);
}
</code></pre>
<h3 id="issue-styling-not-applying">Issue: Styling not applying</h3>
<p><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// 1. Check CSS file is imported</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> <span class="hljs-string">&quot;./Component.css&quot;</span>;

<span class="hljs-comment">// 2. Verify class name matches</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Component: className=&quot;course-card&quot;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// CSS: .course-card { }</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// 3. Check CSS specificity</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// More specific selectors override general ones</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// 4. Use browser DevTools</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Inspect element to see computed styles</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="issue-react-not-rendering">Issue: React not rendering</h3>
<p><strong>Solution:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Check:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// 1. Root element exists: &lt;div id=&quot;root&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// 2. main.jsx renders to correct element</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// 3. No console errors</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// 4. Components return valid JSX</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// 5. Props are correctly passed</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Debug:</span>
<span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Component rendering&quot;</span>, props);
</code></pre>
<h2 id="202-debugging-tips">20.2 Debugging Tips</h2>
<h3 id="react-devtools">React DevTools</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Browser extension for Chrome/Firefox</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// Features:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Inspect component hierarchy</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - View/edit props and state</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Track render reasons</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Time-travel debugging</span>
</code></pre>
<h3 id="console-logging">Console Logging</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Log component renders</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Component mounted&quot;</span>);
  <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Component unmounting&quot;</span>);
}, []);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Log state updates</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> [cart, setCart] = <span class="hljs-title function_">useState</span>([]);
<span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cart:&quot;</span>, cart);

<span class="hljs-comment">// Log effects</span>
<span class="hljs-title function_">useEffect</span>(<span class="hljs-function">() =&gt;</span> {
  <span class="hljs-variable language_">console</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">log</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Cart changed:&quot;</span>, cart);
}, [cart]);
</code></pre>
<h3 id="browser-devtools">Browser DevTools</h3>
<pre><code class="language-javascript"><span class="hljs-comment">// Network Tab:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Monitor HTTP requests</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Check file sizes</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - See load times</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Storage Tab:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Inspect localStorage</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - View cookies</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Check session storage</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Lighthouse:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Performance audit</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Accessibility check</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Best practices</span>

<span class="hljs-comment">// Accessibility Tab:</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Check color contrast</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Verify ARIA labels</span>
<span class="hljs-comment">// - Test keyboard nav</span>
</code></pre>

<h1 id="22-appendix-commands--resources">22. APPENDIX: COMMANDS &amp; RESOURCES</h1>
<h2 id="221-npm-commands">22.1 NPM Commands</h2>
<pre><code class="language-bash"><span class="hljs-comment"># Installation &amp; Dependencies</span>
npm install                    <span class="hljs-comment"># Install all dependencies</span>
npm install package-name       <span class="hljs-comment"># Install specific package</span>
npm update                     <span class="hljs-comment"># Update all packages</span>
npm outdated                   <span class="hljs-comment"># Check for updates</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Development</span>
npm run dev                    <span class="hljs-comment"># Start dev server (localhost:5173)</span>
npm run build                  <span class="hljs-comment"># Build for production</span>
npm run preview                <span class="hljs-comment"># Preview production build</span>
npm run lint                   <span class="hljs-comment"># Check code quality</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Testing</span>
npm run <span class="hljs-built_in">test</span>                   <span class="hljs-comment"># Run all tests</span>
npm run <span class="hljs-built_in">test</span> -- --watch        <span class="hljs-comment"># Run in watch mode</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Git &amp; Deployment</span>
git <span class="hljs-built_in">clone</span> &lt;repo-url&gt;           <span class="hljs-comment"># Clone repository</span>
git add .                      <span class="hljs-comment"># Stage all changes</span>
git commit -m <span class="hljs-string">&quot;message&quot;</span>        <span class="hljs-comment"># Commit changes</span>
git push origin main           <span class="hljs-comment"># Push to GitHub</span>
git pull origin main           <span class="hljs-comment"># Pull from GitHub</span>
</code></pre>

<h1 id="conclusion-1">CONCLUSION</h1>
<h2 id="summary">Summary</h2>
<p>LearnHub is a <strong>comprehensive, production-ready e-learning platform</strong> that demonstrates modern web development practices and patterns. It successfully implements:</p>
<p>✅ <strong>React 19</strong> - Latest framework features and best practices<br>
✅ <strong>State Management</strong> - Context API without Redux complexity<br>
✅ <strong>Responsive Design</strong> - Mobile-first approach working on all devices<br>
✅ <strong>Accessibility</strong> - WCAG 2.1 AA compliant for all users<br>
✅ <strong>Performance</strong> - Optimized with Vite and memoization techniques<br>
✅ <strong>Testing</strong> - Unit tests with Vitest<br>
✅ <strong>Styling</strong> - CSS variables and design tokens for consistency<br>
✅ <strong>Security</strong> - Best practices for data handling<br>
✅ <strong>UX</strong> - Smooth animations and user feedback<br>
✅ <strong>Code Quality</strong> - ESLint and professional architecture</p>

<h1 id="-how-to-convert-to-pdf">📄 HOW TO CONVERT TO PDF</h1>
<h2 id="option-1-using-pandoc-recommended">Option 1: Using Pandoc (Recommended)</h2>
<pre><code class="language-bash"><span class="hljs-comment"># Install pandoc</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># macOS: brew install pandoc</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># Windows: choco install pandoc</span>
<span class="hljs-comment"># Linux: sudo apt-get install pandoc</span>

<span class="hljs-comment"># Convert markdown to PDF</span>
pandoc LEARNHUB_COMPLETE_DOCUMENTATION.md -o LEARNHUB_COMPLETE_DOCUMENTATION.pdf

<span class="hljs-comment"># With styling (more beautiful PDF)</span>
pandoc LEARNHUB_COMPLETE_DOCUMENTATION.md \
  --pdf-engine=xelatex \
  -V mainfont=<span class="hljs-string">&quot;Arial&quot;</span> \
  -o LEARNHUB_COMPLETE_DOCUMENTATION.pdf
</code></pre>
<h2 id="option-2-online-tools-no-installation">Option 2: Online Tools (No Installation)</h2>
<ol>
<li>
<p><strong><a href="http://md-to-pdf.com">md-to-pdf.com</a></strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Upload markdown file</li>
<li>Download PDF</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>markdown.rocks</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Paste markdown content</li>
<li>Export as PDF</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong><a href="http://dillinger.io">dillinger.io</a></strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Write/paste markdown</li>
<li>Export PDF</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="option-3-vs-code-extension">Option 3: VS Code Extension</h2>
<ol>
<li>Install &quot;Markdown PDF&quot; extension</li>
<li>Open markdown file</li>
<li>Right-click → &quot;Markdown PDF: Export (pdf)&quot;</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="option-4-google-docs">Option 4: Google Docs</h2>
<ol>
<li>Create new Google Doc</li>
<li>Paste markdown content</li>
<li>File → Download → PDF</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="option-5-python-script">Option 5: Python Script</h2>
<pre><code class="language-python"><span class="hljs-comment"># Install: pip install markdown-pdf</span>
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> markdown_pdf <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> MarkdownPdf
<span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> pathlib <span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> Path

md_file = Path(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;LEARNHUB_COMPLETE_DOCUMENTATION.md&quot;</span>)
pdf_file = Path(<span class="hljs-string">&quot;LEARNHUB_COMPLETE_DOCUMENTATION.pdf&quot;</span>)

md = MarkdownPdf(md_file)
md.convert(pdf_file)
</code></pre>
